The total expenditure is 1,609,891,000 lire, an increase of 305,000,000 lire compared to the 1935 budget, of which 280,000,000 lire will be used to build new ships. Today, most newspapers here are discussing the issue of the potential for a European war caused by the implementation of an oil embargo against Italy. (National Telegram, 4th)

League of Nations Experts Estimate Italian Oil Reserves; Sufficient to Support Only Seven or Eight Months; Implementation of Oil Embargo Will Be Effective 35

Geneva: The Committee of Experts on the issue of an oil embargo, appointed by the Committee of Eighteen of the League of Nations, has been discussing the five issues determined some time ago (i.e., (1) the oil consumption of Italy and its colonies, (2) its supply situation, (3) its storage volume, (4) its methods of import, (5) its substitutes). After studying the latest statistics, it is known that Italy has begun to stockpile oil since 1934, and it is now estimated that its stockpile reaches one million tons, while its annual consumption needs as much as 1.5 million tons, not including the amount required by the navy. According to people familiar with the oil issue here, the country's oil stockpile can only support seven or eight months. If a small amount of domestic production and sporadic imports from abroad are added, it may be able to support nine or ten months. Therefore, international figures believe that if an oil embargo can be implemented, Italy will be forced to reconsider the issue of peace with Abyssinia before the summer of this year. (Havas, 4th)

Geneva: The Committee of Eighteen of the League of Nations has previously appointed various expert committees to submit reports on the sanctions already implemented by the member states (i.e., arms embargo and financial sanctions), and to study the possibility of implementing an oil embargo. According to information obtained by this agency's reporter, the Committee of Eighteen will generally meet at the end of this month to discuss the above-mentioned reports. The report of the Committee of Experts on the issue of an oil embargo is expected to be drafted by the end of this week. Its content will be purely technical in nature, including the following three points: (1) the amount of oil currently possessed by Italy, (2) the results that the country can obtain by using oil substitutes, (3) the number of oil tankers owned by the country, and the equipment that the country currently has for this oil accumulation. The expert committee will not put forward any conclusions, but will only put forward various facts so that various governments can understand the effects that the implementation of an oil embargo can have. (Havas, 5th)

Geneva: An expert on the oil embargo issue recently made a statement to this agency's reporter, saying that if the US Congress were to veto the new Neutrality Act, the League of Nations might be forced to abandon the proposal to impose an oil embargo on Italy. As far as the current situation is concerned, the US New Neutrality Act has a high probability of being vetoed. In short, even if the oil embargo is implemented, it may not be effective for a certain period of time after its implementation. There are two reasons for this: first, Italy can still use oil substitutes to replace it; second, even if the US Congress passes the New Neutrality Act to facilitate the implementation of the oil embargo, Italy may still be able to undermine this embargo. For this reason, although the Committee of Experts on the issue of an oil embargo appointed by the Committee of Eighteen has begun its work, the final result is still uncertain. (Havas, 5th)

*Pravda* of Soviet Russia Comments: Stance of the Japanese Military: Opposes Fact-Finding by an Investigating Committee 40

Moscow: A dispatch from Tokyo regarding the attitude of the Japanese military authorities toward the Far Eastern Army's proposal, as commented on by *Pravda*, states that if any further proof were needed regarding the fault of the Japanese military authorities in the clash at Grodekovo on the Soviet-Manchukuo border on January 30th and February 1st, it has been provided by the Japanese semi-official organs. According to their reports, the information they released was based on instructions from Japanese military leaders. They deeply fear an impartial investigation of the conflict and dread the conclusion of the Far Eastern Red Army headquarters' announcement, which stated, "Prepared to provide full assistance to any impartial committee coming to investigate the site of the incident." The aforementioned military authorities are now hastily proclaiming that they cannot accept the "proposal of the Far Eastern Red Army" to organize an impartial committee. Clearly, the Far Eastern Red Army headquarters' proposal has deeply alarmed the Japanese military leaders. The reasons they give for opposing the organization of an impartial committee to investigate the January 30th and February 1st incidents are weak and ineffective. They have not provided any proof, nor have they demonstrated what they require. If the Soviet Union had indeed "desired to incite rebellion in Manchukuo to achieve its aggressive aims," then these military leaders, being so fond of peace and justice, could have used this opportunity, through an impartial investigation, to prove the Soviet Union's aggressive behavior. Regarding their claims that the plan to organize a mixed border committee was prevented from being realized by the Soviet Union, this is even more astonishing to those who make such claims. Molotov already pointed out in the previous session of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, "Half a year has passed since our ambassador to Japan, Yurenev, proposed organizing a Soviet-Japanese mixed committee to investigate border incidents, but the Japanese government has yet to respond to this proposal." According to absolutely reliable sources in Moscow, the reason the Japanese government has not responded to the Soviet proposal is due to the obstruction of these military leaders. They are now shifting the responsibility for the failure to establish a mixed committee organization plan to the Soviet government. The purpose of their obstructing the conclusion of an agreement to organize a border committee (a committee that could prevent or restrain border conflicts) is their proposed "demarcation of the national border." They know full well that the Soviet Union will refuse to redraw the border, as the border has already been clearly defined by various treaties. Therefore, the Japanese military, while refusing to organize a border committee, demands the redrawing of the border, is attempting to undermine various methods of adjusting Soviet-Japanese relations and preventing border conflicts, and to maintain the possibility of continuing to carry out provocative atrocities on our border under the false pretext of so-called ambiguous borders. (TASS dispatch, 5th)

Heavy Snowfall in Japan: All Traffic in Tokyo Halted: 20,000 People Mobilized to Clear Snow: Suburban Trains Have Resumed 41

Tokyo: From noon yesterday, heavy snow fell over the Tokyo area, with wind speeds reaching twelve meters per second. Snow continued to fall until midnight this morning. By 9:00 PM last night, the accumulated snow had reached 28.5 centimeters, the heaviest snowfall in forty-nine years. Due to the heavy snow, as many as six hundred streetcars were stranded. Train services on the Tokaido Line were thrown into chaos, and trains were delayed. Streetcars stopped running at 10:00 PM. Only buses were running in the city. All other transportation was cut off. Theaters and movie theaters were deserted. By 10:00 PM, power was also cut off, and the entire city was plunged into darkness. The Tokyo Municipal Bureau of Public Works today mobilized 20,000 workers and 1,000 trucks to carry out snow removal work. Suburban trains have resumed this morning. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

Osaka: Due to the heavy snow since yesterday, ships have encountered disasters in the Seto Inland Sea and elsewhere. The Osaka Shosen Yunnan Maru, fully loaded with grain, was returning from Dalian when it encountered a blizzard off Cape Shio on the morning of the 5th. It sent out a distress signal. Osaka Shosen immediately began rescue operations. When the rescue ship arrived at the scene at 8:30 AM, the ship was nowhere to be seen, and it is feared that it has sunk. The fate of the thirty crew members seems hopeless. The Yunnan Maru weighed 2,210 tons, and the captain was Masaji Saito. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

Tokyo: The entire city of Tokyo has been buried in snow due to the heaviest snowfall in sixty years. All transportation within the city has been cut off. The Municipal Electric Bureau has made every effort to clear the snow from the streetcars and reopened the entire line at 4:00 PM. Normal service will resume on the 6th. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

Gifu: Due to heavy snowfall, transportation in Ibi County, Gifu Prefecture, has been cut off. The Gifu Prefectural Security Team, in cooperation with the police, has been continuously dispatched to the county. The area is covered by fifteen feet of snow. Eighteen houses have been destroyed in Kuse Village. Due to food shortages, people are suffering from hunger and cold. The prefectural authorities are currently taking emergency measures. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

Choshi: A blizzard struck the Choshi area from 8:00 PM on the 4th. The entire city is in darkness. High-voltage power lines have been blown down everywhere, resembling spiderwebs, posing an extreme danger. More than thirty fishing boats have sunk in the harbor, and fourteen docks have collapsed. Three elementary school buildings under construction have also been destroyed. One person has died. Other losses are estimated to be substantial. (Domei dispatch, 5th)

Unable to Find Food in the Snow: Wild Birds Engage in Cannibalism: Millions Fight in the Air 42

Tsuruga: The severe cold and heavy snow in the Hokuriku region, the worst in sixty years, have also caused a major change in the avian world. Because all food on the ground is covered by snow, there is no food to be found. As a result, birds are resorting to cannibalism to alleviate their hunger. Therefore, since the afternoon of the day before yesterday, millions of kites, sparrows, and other birds have been flying in the sky over Tsuruga, engaging in fierce battles. Thousands of dead birds are falling from the sky amidst the white snow. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

The International Ladies' Garment Workers' Union and the Clothing Industry Association have been in negotiations to establish a new agreement regarding wages, but after three months of negotiations, there has been no result, leading the union to announce a stoppage tomorrow. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Slaughterhouse Strike Expands: London Meat Supply Cut Off 44

London: British fresh meat merchants are buying fresh meat from the countryside today to meet demand. The Smithfield slaughterhouse is still on strike, so the supply of fresh meat within a hundred miles of London remains cut off. The previous inventory is only sufficient for London hospitals. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

London: London cold storage workers, in sympathy with the meat market employees, went on strike today. 12,000 are currently on strike, demanding equal pay. Many meat shops have already run out of supplies today. If there are no emergency measures, all butcher shops will have no meat to sell tomorrow. Union leaders have urged the strikers to return to work, but to no avail. The strikers said that negotiations have been ongoing for eight months, but the employers have been dragging their feet, so they had no choice but to strike. The employers believe that this strike is not authorized by the union and will not reopen negotiations unless it ends. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

London: After the cold storage workers went on strike yesterday, the authorities have been working overnight to ensure that Londoners do not suffer from a lack of meat. On the one hand, they have dispatched police to protect the meat market, and on the other hand, they have sent trucks to load meat and distribute it to various cold storage facilities to ensure a continuous supply to retail meat shops. Although the strikers have pickets stationed in various places, there has been no hostile behavior. The authorities have transferred 600 police officers from other locations to central London to prevent disturbances. At night, a truckload of meat attempted to leave the market but was blocked by the strikers. The labor unrest has now spread to the Aldgate meat market, where there are also a hundred strikers. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Swiss National Socialist Party Leader Suddenly Assassinated: The Killer, of Southern Nationality, Surrenders on the Spot: Confesses to Political Motives 45

Davos, Switzerland: The leader of the Swiss branch of the National Socialist Party, Gustloff, was shot dead today by a Yugoslavian Jewish medical student. The assassin, 26 years old, named Frank Furt, went to the police station to surrender after the assassination, claiming that he was not a communist, but he loathed the German National Socialist system, so he intentionally shot and killed Gustloff. The incident occurred this afternoon. The assassin went to Gustloff's residence, spoke a few words with Gustloff, then drew a pistol and fired five shots, killing him. It is said that Gustloff was very active in Switzerland, specializing in gathering information about German expatriates and devising plans to lure Germans living in Switzerland across the border. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Bern, Switzerland: The leader of the Swiss National Socialist Party, Gustloff, was suddenly assassinated at his residence in the city of Davos and died on the spot. The killer, seeing that his goal had been achieved, surrendered to the police tonight. According to his confession, his name is Frank Furt, he is a Yugoslavian, 27 years old, studying medicine in Switzerland. He confessed that the assassination was politically motivated, aiming to strike a blow against National Socialism. Gustloff was a German, proficient in science, and had worked at the Davos Observatory for fourteen years. He was a veteran member of the National Socialist Party and had been very active in Switzerland, gathering German expatriates to organize National Socialist Party groups. He had been fiercely attacked by some socialist newspapers here, demanding that the government order him to leave the country, but the government did not grant the request because Gustloff's activities had not exceeded the bounds of the law. The sudden assassination is feared to have an impact on both Germany and Switzerland. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Berlin: German leader Hitler sent a telegram of condolence to the family of Gustloff, who was assassinated in Switzerland, saying that this act of violence has aroused national indignation. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

U.S. Gold Exports Exceed 9 Million Dollars: 8.5 Million Dollars Shipped to Paris 46

Washington: The U.S. Treasury Department announced that the total value of gold approved for export today was $9,620,000, of which $8,500,000 was shipped to Paris, and the remainder was shipped to the Netherlands. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Washington: Treasury officials stated today that although the U.S. government has $10,182,246,742 in gold reserves, the unencumbered gold is less than $5 billion. It is said that $7,758,000,000 is owned by the Federal Reserve Bank, and $2,000,000,000 is for Federal Reserve note reserves. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

Washington: During the House Appropriations Committee's study of the Treasury Department's budget, Chairman Buchanan, a Democratic member of the House, expressed doubts about the success of the Treasury Department's silver purchase plan. Buchanan said, "I know that it is very good to purchase enough silver to achieve an appropriate ratio of gold to silver, but a foundation must first be established so that the commercial nations of the world can use the bimetallic standard. Now that the Treasury Department cannot achieve this goal, I truly do not know what benefit there is in buying silver, other than raising the price of silver in some silver-producing areas in the country." Beforehand, Director of the Budget and Undersecretary of the Treasury Bell had also stated that the silver purchase plan was not making progress. Buchanan then asked the Treasury Department how much more silver it needed to purchase to achieve a gold-to-silver ratio of 3:1. Bell replied, "This is difficult to calculate, because the Treasury Department's cash reserves are also increasing at the same time as it purchases silver, so progress is very slow, and it is still far away." Treasury Secretary Morgenthau informed Buchanan that the silver purchase law was an "absolute order," so it could not be stopped until the goal of a gold-to-silver ratio of 3:1 was achieved. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

U.S. Senate Passes Bill to Repeal Cotton Production Control Act: Also Passes Two Other Control Acts 47

Washington: Based on President Roosevelt's overall message, the Senate today passed a bill to repeal the Bankhead Cotton Control Act, the Kerr-Smith Tobacco Act, and the Potato Control Act. This resolution has now been sent to the House. The Senate will also begin debating the government's agricultural bill tomorrow to replace the Agricultural Adjustment Act, which the Supreme Court ruled unconstitutional. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

Washington: President Roosevelt announced today that he has ordered the cancellation of government loans, as the situation has gradually recovered, so there is no need to grant such large loans anymore. The President added that this action is not immediately a government austerity policy. However, the financial community is paying close attention to this order, given the recent propaganda of inflation, the weakness of the dollar exchange rate, and the opposition of Congress to new taxes, etc. The President explained that this move is not to "recall" funds that have already been designated, but to cancel the amounts previously approved. For example, the Home Owners' Loan Corporation has now become a collection agency and no longer needs to grant loans. At the same time, President Roosevelt announced that he has convened the heads of various relief agencies to meet tomorrow, leading some to speculate that federal government spending may be greatly reduced. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

Washington: Political circles close to Congress stated today that the House's propaganda of inflation will fail due to opposition in the Senate or a veto by the President. Even though the atmosphere of inflation is strong, even if the President vetoes it, the House may not be able to get two-thirds of the Senate to override the President's veto. At the same time, the Federal Reserve Board will visit Treasury Secretary Morgenthau today, at which time they will discuss the financial situation and issues such as inflation. Although the Federal Reserve has the power to control credit inflation, it has no power to interfere with currency inflation. Observers familiar with the situation believe that while President Roosevelt opposes currency inflation, the United States may not be able to avoid credit inflation. The huge deposits in banks now may flow into the real economy and encounter a boom similar to the era of President Coolidge. Some experts believe that credit inflation and currency inflation are equally dangerous, the difference being that the latter is triggered immediately, while the former waits to explode later. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

Hungary: Communist Organization Smashed: Fifteen Leaders Arrested 48

Budapest, Hungary: In the past few weeks, the capital's detective team has been paying attention to communist activities and is currently destroying the Communist headquarters. Fifteen leaders have been arrested. The cracking of this case proves that the previous suspicion that communist propaganda was produced by experts. Among those arrested is West Keiss, who is well-known in Hungary because he participated in the Soviet dictatorship in Soviet Russia in 1927 and is on the wanted list. Keiss was convicted and imprisoned at that time, then escaped to Soviet Russia, and was sent back to the country by Soviet Russia under the guise of a low-ranking cadre. Bela Kun had used the most brutal means to organize the Hungarian Communist Party and rebel against the government. The evidence obtained this time shows that all the current disputes are related to Bela Kun in Moscow. One of his accomplices is Dr. Veilu, a most prestigious physician in the capital's sanatorium. In the underground room of Dr. Veilu's residence, not only were countless propaganda items hidden, but also many false passports, communist lists, various reports sent to Moscow, and large amounts of foreign currency. According to detectives, there was a special envoy coming and going when Moscow entered the Hungarian capital, so this organization can also be said to be performing military espionage work at the same time. The remaining arrested leaders include a well-known artist, a senior insurance company executive, a female doctor, and a vocational school lecturer. (Kokumin dispatch, 4th)

How to Improve Students' Math Scores? Professor Ren Mengxian of Great China University (Part 2) 49

(Lecture to Secondary School Students Nationwide on January 14th and 16th)

Based on several relative principles in mathematics teaching—synthesis and analysis, deduction and induction, reasoning and experimentation...different theories have formed various teaching methods: such as (a) examination style, which makes students familiar with the assigned teaching materials, and teachers can evaluate their merits through quizzes or written tests; (b) recitation style, which allows students to demonstrate what they have learned, either by reciting theorems or summarizing and presenting, and teachers can point out right and wrong at any time; (c) lecture style, which allows students to listen to the teacher's lectures, with everything centered on the teacher's actions; (d) discussion style, which allows students to openly discuss problems, with the teacher only acting as the chairman; (e) individual guidance style, which allows students to seek guidance from the teacher based on their own insights or questions, and the teacher provides individualized guidance according to their needs; (f) self-discovery style, which allows students to conduct further research based on their existing knowledge, striving for self-discovery; (g) group experimentation style, which divides students into small groups to obtain necessary new knowledge through practical observation and testing, similar to other natural sciences.

These are all teaching methods used by mathematics teachers in the classroom, but which one is the most suitable? Let's compare them now.

(1) Styles a, b, and c These three styles, although said to be rigid, passive, and restrictive to the spirit for students, seem unsuitable for teaching, but if used well, each has its effectiveness.

(1) Advantages of effectively using the examination style: (I) It can cultivate students' habit of independent study, so that they do not rely on the teacher for everything; (II) It can make students not afraid of trouble and work patiently; (III) It can arouse students' competitive spirit, thereby promoting their progress.

(2) Advantages of effectively using the recitation style: (I) It can use the opportunity of performance to correct students' errors in language and writing. It is a common and unavoidable fact that mathematics teachers fulfill the obligation of revising students' language and writing on behalf of Chinese and even foreign language teachers. (II) It can enable students to gradually develop their creative abilities in the practice of retelling. For example, students can be asked to explain the propositions related to solid angles by comparing them with the theorems of plane triangles. (III) It can provide a clear and confident concept for students with relatively vague understanding and scattered thinking, such as the properties of the nine-point circle, the formula for the sine or cosine of a half angle. The proof procedure is relatively tight, so students may be asked to reprove it once.

(3) Advantages of effectively using the lecture style: (I) It is convenient for systematic or regular narration, such as the classified presentation of solutions to simultaneous equations—from addition and subtraction to elimination...to expansion using determinants. (II) It is convenient to conclude matters that have already been explained above, such as making a general discussion after calculating the numerical values of the roots of a quadratic equation separately. (III) It is convenient to extract outlines and clearly indicate summaries, such as pointing out that the propositions of spatial planes and lines are nothing more than parallel and perpendicular relationships. (IV) It is convenient to compare in many ways, making the results clearer, such as comparing the methods of finding the surface area and volume of cylinders and cones with those of prisms and pyramids, which can best make students' concepts clear. (V) It is convenient to review known things, making it easier for students to accept newly taught theories, such as reviewing the properties of spherical geometry before teaching spherical trigonometry.

(2) Styles d, e, and f These three styles, although said to be flexible, automatic, and adapted to personality for students, seem quite suitable for teaching, but if not used well, each has its drawbacks.

(1) Disadvantages of not using the discussion style well: (I) Learning opportunities are difficult to equalize. (II) Students' expressions of thought may not come from true knowledge and insight, and it is easy to develop opportunistic and cunning malpractices. (III) Arguments change at every turn, often causing unnecessary disputes.

(2) Disadvantages of not using the individual guidance style well: (I) There is a lack of opportunities for the cultivation of group spirit, such as common mistakes, which cannot be universally brought to their attention. (II) Students are unwilling to make efforts automatically, often resorting to hypocrisy and settling for laziness. (III) Teachers work harder, but students benefit limitedly, because if the number of people is too large, there is not enough time to allocate.

(3) Disadvantages of not using the self-discovery style well: (I) Time is particularly uneconomical. (II) It is not suitable for more difficult or abstract problems, such as the exploration of the properties of integers, etc. (III) It is not suitable for lower grades or when starting to learn a certain subject, such as when reading geometry for the first time, with nothing to rely on, how can one learn new things by reviewing the old?

(3) Group Experimentation Style The purpose of using this teaching method is to concretize various theorems and methods in mathematics, just like physics, chemistry, and biology. It is indeed a latest trend, but the problems that still need to be studied include:

(1) Allocation of experimental materials such as the observation, measurement, and use of physical objects and figures; the creation and correction of calculation tables; and the application of graphs are all experimental materials. But how should these materials be allocated reasonably?

(2) Design of experimental procedures such as how to make experimental films

(3) Equipment of experimental tools such as ordinary tools, calculation tools, measurement tools, geometric models, and physical instruments are all necessary tools for experimentation. But how should they be equipped to be applicable?

From the above comparison, which teaching method is the best in space? How should it be chosen? My point is:

(1) Teaching methods become more refined through research, and vary according to the object. There is no fixed format, nor is there an absolute evaluation of excellence.

(2) Teaching methods obtained through meticulous research and practical experience are more meaningful and applicable.

(3) When adopting any method, it is necessary to be active at all times and make multiple connections, and avoid partiality and clinging to one kind.

(4) The standard for selection should be determined by the benefits obtained by the students and the results they show. The teacher's own convenience should not be considered.

As for whether or not to correct students' exercise books, or how to correct them? These after-class processing methods are considered difficult problems to solve by any teacher. According to the current treatment of middle school teachers, the teaching hours of teachers often exceed 20 hours per week, which means that they often teach four classes of students, with a total number of about 150 or 160 people. Now, if exercise books are collected once a week for each class, and each book has about 20 questions, then the teacher must correct at least 3,000 questions per week. If each question is assumed to take half a minute, it will take no less than 25 hours. Therefore, if teachers correct exercise books, in addition to teaching, the effort spent on after-class processing averages more than four hours per day, not to mention the preparation of teaching materials, research on teaching methods, and reviewing test papers. Therefore, insufficient time is already a major obstacle to solving this problem; moreover, exercise books are not easy to collect, and their contents often have the drawbacks of plagiarism and similarity; and it is not yet known whether students pay attention to reviewing after correction. Therefore, some people say that correcting exercise books wastes a great deal of labor for teachers, and the result is proofreading for students who plagiarize, which does not enable them to do the exercises. However, how students learn mathematics, I said before, cannot be done without sufficient practice; and the improvement of students' grades depends entirely on the teacher's detailed guidance on a daily basis; and since students have been urged to do the exercises, what is the point of not correcting them? Therefore, the collection and correction of exercise books are necessary, for the sake of teaching effectiveness and student progress, there is no doubt. But whether it is possible for teachers to correct depends on whether teachers can flexibly use the correction method and whether they have legitimate teaching and appropriate training for students. Such as

(1) To alleviate the difficulty of insufficient correction time, teachers can select one-third or one-quarter of all exercise books (or all the exercises in each book) for detailed correction after collecting the exercise books, and the rest can be briefly reviewed, and then the one-third or one-quarter can be corrected in detail next time. By correcting in this way in turn, teachers can save at least half of the time, and students can get the benefit of five or even six detailed corrections per semester. Why should teachers be afraid not to do it? But once collected, it must be returned in the shortest possible time. Otherwise, the students have forgotten how a certain question should be calculated after a long time. Although the teacher's correction is detailed, the students do not pay attention.

(2) Supervise students to practice on time, and eliminate the drawbacks of mutual plagiarism. Teachers must have a definite study on teaching methods. On weekdays, they have cultivated students' habits of previewing, and do not allow them to be neglected; they also value class work, and do not allow them to give up; and they carefully select useful exercises, and do not make them excessive; then students will be happy to accept the teacher's instructions, and practice tirelessly. Teachers also strictly stipulate examination methods. In the event of unconscious plagiarism, both parties will be canceled at the same time, and then the cultivation of the mind will be carried out. On the one hand, the interest of students in striving for progress will be aroused, and on the other hand, the concept of independent self-help will be cultivated to develop the spirit of truthfulness and integrity. Then students will be ashamed of plagiarism, and the effect of the so-called unity of teaching and training can be realized here!

Third, the expression of spirit Education is a spiritual career. If you want students to have good grades, teachers must have rich knowledge and appropriate teaching methods, and they must also have a full spirit. There are three aspects to the expression of spirit:

(1) Interest Students learn mathematics, they must have a good interest. Teachers teach mathematics, they must have a better interest. Ordinary people who engage in a profession often complain about one line in another line. If teachers also have this tendency, it will have a great impact on the students' minds. Therefore, teachers must have a professional interest and a love of work. Since they have already taken this as a career, they should concentrate on it and not have other thoughts.

(2) Attitude Whether the teacher's meaning can be exercised on the students does not depend on the teacher's strictness in supervision, but on whether the teacher's attitude can win the students' belief. Therefore, the teacher's attitude must be (1) solemn and upright fair treatment, lawful treatment, lawful and not biased. (2) Tense pace, responsible for things. (3) Sincere and patient persuasion, with sympathy.

(3) Physique A full spirit resides in a healthy physique; and the task cannot be accomplished without the physical strength to take on others. Therefore, teachers' physiques must pay attention to exercise, so that they are healthy and strong, then the work can be completed, and it can also be a model for students

To summarize what has been said above, my conclusion is:

(1) An ideal teacher must have strength and also have methods.

(2) Only with strength can there be methods. Teachers with insufficient strength, no matter how many methods they have, are ineffective.

(3) Only teachers with noble personality and full spirit can use their methods, develop their strength, and complete the purpose of teaching.

Hu Hanmin in Guangdong, Meeting with People from All Walks of Life, Visiting Military and Political Organs and Comrades, Delivering Profound Admonitions to Party Members 80

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Mr. Hu Hanmin arrived in Guangdong, various heads of organs and representatives stationed in Guangdong have been vying to pay their respects, but he has been unable to receive them. On January 30, he received heads of party, political, and military organs and committee members at the Southwest Political Affairs Committee. At 9:30 in the morning, everyone gathered, including Li Zongren, Chen Jitang, Lin Yunkai, Zou Lu, Liu Jiwen, as well as committee members of the provincial and municipal governments, heads of various departments and bureaus, executive and supervisory committee members of the provincial and municipal party headquarters, and senior officials of the Southwest Executive Department and the Southwest Political Council, totaling more than fifty people. Hu then expressed his long-held views on the party and the country, followed by speeches by Chen Jitang and Li Zongren. The meeting adjourned at about 11:00. After the meeting, Hu rode to the headquarters of the First Group Army to visit the senior officers of the headquarters, conversing for twenty minutes before taking his leave. He then went to the provincial government, where Lin Yunkai and Liu Jiwen led the heads of various departments and bureaus of the provincial government to greet him respectfully. Hu inquired in detail about the three-year administrative plan and various new constructions in Guangdong province, which Lin Yunkai and Liu Jiwen explained separately. At 11:50, Hu received representatives of overseas party branches and representatives of various provinces in Guangdong at the Western-style flower hall of the provincial government. More than a hundred representatives were present, and committee members of the Southwest Executive Department and the provincial and municipal party headquarters also participated. Hu immediately stood up and delivered a speech, elaborating on his own views on the party and the country. His admonition was as follows:

"I have been away from the province for more than four years. I am very pleased to meet with you comrades here today. Since arriving in the province, I have spoken a little too much and feel slightly tired. Therefore, I have followed the doctor's advice for the past two days and rested a bit, which has delayed the meeting. I apologize for this. All of you comrades present are party affairs workers, so what I say today will also focus on party affairs. I hope you will carefully consider it. When I decided to return to the country, I received a warm welcome from comrades and compatriots in Guangdong and Hong Kong. The enthusiasm of this welcome is unprecedented. I have often said that this may be 'the meaning of love me, love my dog.' They are concerned about the crisis of the country and eagerly hope that people like me, who have always cared about national affairs, can resolve it. Therefore, the welcome of comrades and compatriots to me and the problems they seek to solve mainly fall into two categories. The more urgent and temporary one is how to resolve diplomacy, and the more gradual and long-term one is how to reorganize party affairs. When I was in Europe, comrades at home and abroad asked me about this one after another. I told them with two sentences: 'The party should be restored to a party with principles and spirit, and the government should be reformed into a government with responsibility and ability.' If we talk about the party in terms of the party, then our party has only a shell left, without any so-called principles and spirit. When the Premier created the party, he first called it the 'Chinese Revolutionary Alliance,' then the 'Chinese Revolutionary Party,' then the 'Kuomintang,' and finally today's 'Chinese Kuomintang.' Its essence is 'revolution,' and 'Chinese Nationals.' The Three Principles of the People invented by the Premier are: first, nationalism; second, democracy; and third, people's livelihood, all of which are closely related to the 'people' of the nation. Therefore, the Chinese Kuomintang is actually a 'Chinese National Salvation Party' or a 'Chinese People's Salvation Party.' Every party member must go deep into the people and carry out the principle of saving the country to conform to the original meaning of the Chinese Kuomintang. However, the current situation is not like this. People who criticize our party say, 'I only see party headquarters, but I don't see party members.' I would go further and say, 'I only see committee members, but I don't see party members. Whether there are party headquarters is still questionable.' If the party has no party members, or the party has party members, but in fact, it is as if they have lost their existence, then this so-called party has actually lost its substance. The Premier built the party to build the country and even to govern the country. Therefore, the Chinese Kuomintang is the key to initiating all revolutions. I have always advocated that to save the country, we must first save the party. What is the party? To put it plainly, it is to gather comrades who believe in the Three Principles of the People under an organization, pool our wisdom and efforts, and fight for the principles. Therefore, to become a party member, to become a comrade, the only essence is 'sacrifice' and 'obligation.' Since the Alliance Association, our party has used this spirit to overthrow the Manchu Qing and establish the Republic of China. At that time, if comrades were not careful, their lives and property would be sacrificed. Therefore, party members were mostly people with outstanding ambitions and firm integrity. At the beginning of joining the party, they had already decided to devote their lives to the party and the country. The past spirit of our party is vastly different from the past reality. 'Obligation' is changed to 'right,' and 'sacrifice' is changed to 'seizure.' The spirit is lost, only the form remains, and the promotion of the principles is no longer hoped for. Today, the country is in danger, but the party comrades are lax and indulge in pleasure, almost forgetting their duties to the party and the country, and the spirit of sacrifice and dedication. It is truly a great danger to the country. I have been in Europe for six months, all in remote villages, just recuperating. However, in Germany and Italy, I also carefully examined their party affairs. Although their principles are different, and the national situations are different, the tense and serious spirit of their party members is far beyond what our party can achieve. The ancients said, 'In the affairs of the people, take the lead in your own person, and defend them with your own person.' Revolutionary party members should all be like this. The party members in Germany and Italy do have this kind of image. Their tasks are more important than ordinary people's, their work is more complicated than ordinary people's, and they have no power. The party's principles and spirit are expressed in this way. In Germany, when the party issued an order that each party comrade should only eat one piece of meat per meal for the sake of frugality, the party members advocated it, and the whole people followed it, so that restaurants everywhere only sold one piece per customer per day, and no one failed to comply with it. Although this is a small matter, its discipline and spirit are truly admirable. Just from this one point, we can generalize the rest. The so-called taking the lead and working hard, there is nowhere that they do not go to the extreme. I ask, can our party do this? If our party cannot create this kind of ethos and restore the spirit of sacrifice and struggle of the Alliance Association era, the principles will have no way to be promoted, and the party and the country will have no way to be saved. I have compared the party to an army, meaning that it must be like an army, becoming more and more refined through training. I have also compared the party to a congenital state, meaning that it must be built into a future state with a spirit of order and seriousness based on a certain direction. I have also compared the party to a school, meaning that comrades are like classmates, and their research on revolutionary principles and exploration of revolutionary strategies can be new day by day and month by month. I have also compared it to a family, meaning that comrades can be loving and sincere to each other, trust each other, and help each other, and work hard for revolutionary work. I deeply believe that only in this way can the party have life, can the principles be promoted, and can the country have hope of revival. Therefore, the body and spirit of a person may sometimes decline, but the life of the party must become more and more abundant. Guangdong is the revolutionary base of our party. I think back to the difficulty of creating our party and the hardship of the Premier's dedication to the revolution. All kinds of hardships were personally experienced by me. Therefore, I especially want to express my deep expectations for the reorganization of party affairs. I sincerely hope that the party affairs workers in this province and city can understand the original meaning of the creation of this party, deeply observe the current crisis of this party, carefully examine the current tasks of this party, and, based on the meaning of 'Please start with me,' strive to reform, so that the reorganization of this party's party affairs can start from this. This is my hope." (January 30)

General Supervisor Chiang's Speech: The Mission of the Anti-Smoking Association; Remarks at a Meeting of the Anti-Smoking Association 81

Nanjing News: The Anti-Smoking Association held its first meeting on February 1. General Supervisor Chiang attended and delivered a speech entitled "The Mission of the Anti-Smoking Association." The original text of the speech is recorded below:

"I just heard Secretary-General Li (Jihong) report on the progress of anti-smoking in recent years. Although there has been progress year by year, it has never achieved the expected results according to the original plan. This is something I feel very ashamed of and very sorry for the country. Today, national leaders from all walks of life have gathered here to discuss anti-smoking at this critical moment for the rise and fall of the nation. I will take this opportunity to offer a few personal opinions.

The Danger of Opium is Greater Than Foreign Aggression 82

Everyone knows that opium must be banned, and the continued implementation of the ban has been going on for a long time. However, because anti-smoking has never been thoroughly done in the past, people generally regard it as commonplace. On the one hand, they always say that opium must be eradicated, and on the other hand, they always think that it is very difficult or even impossible to eradicate opium. It is because of this contradictory psychology and reality that people who handle anti-smoking affairs often start with great enthusiasm, determination, and courage, but later gradually become passive and discouraged, and even end up with no results. Therefore, if we want to eradicate opium in the future, the first thing we must do is to break this old and wrong concept, to recognize that opium can definitely be eradicated, and to be determined by ourselves to thoroughly eradicate it. Secondly, there is another common misconception that the current crisis of the country is first foreign aggression and second opium. However, foreign aggression is external invasion and oppression, while opium is internal degeneration and suicide. Therefore, in terms of the nature of the situation, opium is many times more dangerous than foreign aggression. Moreover, the coming of foreign aggression is due to our own internal chaos, corruption, and weakness. If we can be determined to cultivate our spirit, revitalize our spirit, improve our internal affairs, and enhance our national strength, there are of course many active construction projects to be done. However, due to the limitations of talent and material resources, it is often not easy to carry out active construction projects. Therefore, on the negative side, removing the ills is the way to promote benefits, which is also a way to achieve twice the result with half the effort. When it comes to negative removal, the most urgent and important thing is of course to ban smoking. If anti-smoking is not effective, all other political construction work, no matter how hard we try, will not be effective. Therefore, we must all see the danger of opium as greater than foreign aggression, and recognize that eradicating opium is the first priority for improving internal affairs and revitalizing the country.

Concerning National and Ethnic Personality 83

The importance of anti-smoking is such, but the agencies that have been in charge of anti-smoking in the past have often been nominal or have started strictly but ended loosely. They started with more serious work and stricter bans, but later gradually declined and eventually became completely equivalent to non-ban. We cannot say that this common situation has completely disappeared until recently. The establishment of our Anti-Smoking Association this time can be said to be the final test of whether China's anti-smoking can succeed, and it is also the most recent test of whether the personality of our nation and country can stand in the international community. Because the international community wants to see what other people can do, whether we can do it, and whether we can put into practice what we say. In short, it wants to see whether our nation and country have a noble personality of independence and self-reliance. It only needs to see whether our country can eradicate opium from now on. Therefore, if we want to win personality for the nation and the country, we must ban smoking as soon as possible.

Government and People Work Together 84

Gentlemen, you have always sacrificed everything to seek national and people's welfare. Of course, you have special enthusiasm for anti-smoking. As for the government, I dare to be responsible for stating that the government has absolutely no intention of collecting taxes in disguise or extending the tax period for any financial convenience. The government's intention is absolutely to find a perfect and effective way to achieve the goal of eradicating opium and eliminating smoking as soon as possible. However, because the situation in China in all aspects is relatively special, it is indeed not easy to thoroughly achieve the goal of anti-smoking if we rely solely on the government's efforts. Because there are many places, (especially the concessions in Shanghai, Hankou, and Tianjin) and many situations, (especially foreigners selling drugs in China) that the government's power cannot fully reach. Therefore, in many situations, it is more effective to rely on the power of society than to rely solely on the power of the government to ban smoking. If the leaders of all walks of life in the society can take responsibility for anti-smoking and work together, this power will be ten times greater than that of the government. For example, there are more than twenty gentlemen present today. If each person can directly or indirectly fulfill the responsibility of propaganda, persuasion, supervision, and execution, whether at home or abroad, whether to the government or the people, this power will definitely be more powerful than that of ordinary two hundred thousand people. Therefore, I hope that everyone can carefully discuss a perfect plan at this meeting. In the future, everyone should assist the government to work together consistently, with the greatest effort, to declare war on opium, in order to achieve the goal of eradication.

Assist All Provinces to Eradicate Thoroughly 85

Again, we have made progress every year in anti-smoking recently. In addition to the special effectiveness of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, the tobacco planting areas in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the northwest provinces have also been sharply reduced. Even in Sichuan, which used to produce a lot of tobacco, the area allowed to grow tobacco has also been reduced from more than a dozen counties to ten counties. However, we must know that in order to maintain these achievements, especially to achieve the goal of thorough anti-smoking throughout the country, the government and leaders from all walks of life in society must continue to step up their efforts. In particular, we believe that the highest officials in many places are definitely not greedy for tax revenue, but in fact, they lack active determination and cannot use a pragmatic spirit to eradicate opium. Especially in remote provinces, they do not know that the interior has been strictly banned, so it is inevitable. If this situation cannot be changed, no matter how hard our Anti-Smoking Association works, I am afraid that most of the work will be equal to empty talk on paper and will be difficult to achieve practical results. Gentlemen, you all have a long-standing reputation in various places and in all walks of life. I hope you will pay special attention to this point, and encourage and assist the chairmen of all provinces, especially the local officials in remote provinces, directly or indirectly, publicly or privately, so that they can increase their active spirit and make special efforts in anti-smoking in the future. As for the Anti-Smoking Supervision Office, which is supervised by this association and is in charge of anti-smoking, we must of course supervise it more closely to prevent any favoritism and to fulfill its duties. In addition, with regard to the international aspect, especially the concessions in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and other places, the foreigners directly and indirectly manufacturing and selling drugs are beyond the reach of our government's power. We can only do our best to arouse the sympathy of international public opinion and use the power of society and morality to prevent and control them, so that foreigners who sell drugs for profit will not dare to blatantly commit criminal acts.

Greatest Determination to Complete Work 86

Finally, on the government side, as the President of the Executive Yuan and concurrently the General Supervisor of Anti-Smoking, I am of course the most responsible. I have just said that anti-smoking is the first priority for improving our internal affairs. If anti-smoking is not effective, it can be said that any other political construction is fake and cannot take effect. Therefore, whether anti-smoking can be effective in the future can also test the strength of our political power and can measure the success or failure of our political construction. On the one hand, I encourage myself with this, and on the other hand, I also hope that you gentlemen will especially supervise and assist the government, with unity from top to bottom, to work together, and achieve the expected results according to the scheduled time limit. In short, now, in order to complete the political construction of the revolution, in order to save the country and the nation from danger, in order to establish a noble personality for the nation and the country, and in order to improve the status of the nation and the country, opium must be eradicated as soon as possible. If we want to eradicate opium, on the one hand, the government must of course bear the greatest responsibility and make the greatest effort. On the other hand, it is even more necessary to increase the active determination of the responsible authorities in all parts of the country, to stir up the enthusiastic sympathy of all friendly countries, and to awaken the universal awareness of the people of the whole country. Then, with the same heart and the same virtue at home and abroad, with the greatest determination and courage, according to a perfect and effective plan, we will mobilize the whole body, work together, complete the work of anti-smoking, establish the highest personality of our country, and make it the basis for our national revival. This is the great significance of our opening ceremony today. I encourage myself with this, and I also encourage all of you gentlemen. I hope that everyone will fulfill their responsibilities and complete the mission of the entire association."

Songjiang: Handling the Registration of Smokers for Self-Renewal

This county is handling the registration of smokers for self-renewal. After the Inspection Committee member Mr. Ren Yingcang, entrusted by the department, and County Chief Yang agreed on various methods to promote the registration of smokers for self-renewal in various districts, they are implementing them step by step, and the results are quite effective. However, in the first district, which belongs to the urban area, the number of registered people during the general registration period is ten times more than that in the rural areas. Therefore, this time, after District Chief Shen Fuyun personally went out to investigate and squeeze, he also reached more than 500 people. It can be seen that the omissions in each district are quite considerable. Therefore, County Chief Li personally went to various townships in the north and south of Pu to carry out investigations and squeezes, and at the same time examined the progress of general administration in various district offices.

Jiading: Four Robbers Captured in Huangdu

At about 8:00 p.m. on the 3rd, four robbers in plain clothes went to the Zhengda Rice Store in the west market of Huangdu to rob. Because the store hid the secrets of banknotes, they failed and left. The store owner, Wu Bosheng, reported the information to the town public office of the town. The provincial security team stationed in the town and the water police team were dispatching teams to search. When the robbers passed by the Jinshiji Rice Store in the east market, they re-entered to rob and robbed 40 yuan in cash and fled east. According to the store owner Jin Shijun's continuous report, the town public office telegraphed the Second Sub-bureau of the South Gate Public Security Bureau. As a result, the police station captured a robber named Wu Shaotang at the West Yangliu Bridge of Huangxiang Station. The Public Security Sub-bureau captured three robbers named Chen Xiaolong, Chen Deming, and Zhu Qingcai in Zhujia Village and escorted them to the Nanxiang Public Security Sub-bureau. They also found silver notes and other items in their trouser legs. On the 4th, they ordered the client Jin Shijun to go to the bureau to identify the banknotes found. Among the banknotes, there was a 5-yuan counterfeit note, which was indeed the original stolen goods. According to the confession, they had a pistol, which they threw into the river in a hurry. Director Zheng of the sub-bureau prepared a document with the information obtained and submitted it to the county for investigation.

Kunshan: Key Criminals Captured in Wusongjiang Robbery Case

Mao Weisou, a senator of the Military Senate, moved from Shanghai to Suzhou on December 24 of last year. He hired a boat to transport goods. At about 8:00 p.m. on the 28th, when he arrived at the mouth of the Wusong River in this county, he suddenly encountered more than a dozen bandits who swarmed onto the boat, intending to rob. A bandit was shot dead by the bodyguard. Seeing that the situation was not good, the remaining bandits jumped into the water and fled. Afterwards, the case was reported to the county public security bureau for strict arrest. The bandits Wu Xiaotuzi and his wife Xue, Chen Jiaxing and other three people were arrested. It was found that there were also accomplices Wang Dalunzi hiding in the Nanshi area of Shanghai. After the detective Li sent officers to arrest the fugitive Wang Dalunzi in Nanshi, he was escorted to Kunshan for interrogation.

Wuxi: American Merchants Claim Compensation for Loss of Inferior Silk

Last year, the price of Chinese silk was active in Europe, and the market improved, so silk factories in Shanghai and Wuxi both made huge profits. However, some reeling factories only focused on rough manufacturing and did not care about overseas credit, resulting in poor quality products. Now, various American silk factories and sock factories have purchased this Chinese silk, which has had a huge impact. They have sent letters to the American Blue Yu Bi Foreign Firm, the manager of American silk exports stationed in Shanghai, claiming compensation for losses of US$87,000, equivalent to about 260,000 Chinese currency. After receiving the letter, the foreign firm turned to the Wuxi and Shanghai silk factory trade associations to negotiate compensation. At the same time, the Wuxi Silk Factory Association received a letter of warning from the secretary of the Shanghai Foreign Merchants Export Raw Silk Association, saying that the B-grade white silk produced by the French Lyon was of the worst quality, which hindered production. All silk and sock factories hated it. If they do not pay close attention to improvement in the future, they will have to buy Japanese raw silk, because Japanese silk is guaranteed to be reliable and is improving year by year. This is a hidden worry for the future of Chinese silk.

The Jiahu Highway is very important for transportation between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The road bureau has been actively rushing to build it. The earthwork has been completed, and the bridges and road surface are still in progress. It is now planned to invite merchants to lease the road, as the total project is limited to be completed by the end of this month, and the construction funds are insufficient. The business of the road will be used as collateral, and 350,000 yuan will be borrowed from the merchants. The lease period of the road is about 20 years. A contract has been drafted. Once agreed upon, it can be signed and established.

Economic Anecdotes 87

— Tang Qingzeng

The Accountant Profession in China (Part 1) 88

— Xu Yongzuo

(I) What is an Accountant? Although the title of "accountant" has become familiar to the public in recent years, the general public still lacks a deep understanding of the duties and functions of an accountant. Some believe that accountants are only responsible for exposing fraud and errors in accounts, while others think that accountants merely handle the aftermath of bankrupt businesses, such as liquidation. Both of these assumptions are misunderstandings.

These two misunderstandings are greatly detrimental to the status of accountants in society. If we reason based on these two misunderstandings, then commercial and industrial enterprises with no fraudulent or erroneous accounts, or those not facing bankruptcy and liquidation, would see no crucial need to hire an accountant. As a result, accountants would become an inauspicious presence, leading people to avoid contact or socializing with them, fearing that such interactions might suggest impending misfortune for their businesses.

As mentioned above, if the accountant profession were limited to investigating and exposing fraudulent or erroneous accounts, or to liquidating bankrupt businesses, its role would be confined to the passive sphere. However, this is far from the truth. While a significant portion of accounting work is passive, the majority is actually active. We must understand that accountants should be engaged before any fraud or errors occur in the accounts, and while the business is still operating, so that their design and guidance can help the business thrive. This does not mean that the passive function of accountants is not beneficial to society, but rather that it is less significant than their active function and should not be overemphasized.

In the past, when hiring accountants in England, their remuneration was often determined by the number of frauds they uncovered. However, this is no longer the case. As businesses have expanded in scale and become more complex in their organizational structure, they have been able to adopt strict internal control systems, greatly reducing the opportunity for fraud and error, thus eliminating the need for accountants to simply uncover wrongdoings. Consequently, the role of accountants has shifted towards verifying financial status and preventing fraud and errors. Through audits and certifications, accountants ensure that financial statements accurately reflect the true financial position and operating results. Furthermore, through design and recommendations, they ensure that systems and facilities are effective in preventing fraud and errors. From this, we can see that the role of accountants initially focused on the passive aspects but has recently shifted towards the active. A certain British scholar once said, "An accountant should rather be a watchdog than a hunting dog," which conveys this very idea.

However, the mission of an accountant is not merely to prevent irregularities. Their greatest task lies in analyzing the development trends of a business and guiding its management policies, enabling it to thrive on a sound path. This impacts the success or failure of a single enterprise, as well as the prosperity or decline of the entire national economy. Is their effectiveness not significant? Therefore, it can be said that accountants are to commercial and industrial enterprises as doctors are to human life. If you only seek a doctor's advice when you are already sick or critically ill, it is too late. Thus, we can define the accountant profession as follows: "Accounting is a specialized profession that focuses on the organization and design before an accounting event, the temporary calculation and recording during the event, and the analysis and audit after the event."

The functional effectiveness of accountants is as described above. However, in our country, the accountant profession is still quite nascent. Compared to the United States and Britain, it is similar to their situation forty or fifty years ago, and the opportunities for using accountants in society are still biased towards the passive aspects, which is regrettable. In reality, at this time when the social economy is in a state of panic and business operations are facing difficulties, we should make full use of accountants to bring their active functions into play, supporting the commercial and industrial sectors to move towards a stable and healthy path.

(II) Accountant Qualifications To be an accountant, one must possess sufficient knowledge and experience. Therefore, most countries have relatively strict requirements for the qualifications of accountants. Let us first discuss the systems in the United States and Britain.

The United States and Britain have stricter requirements for accountant qualifications, especially Britain. In Britain, accountants are mainly trained by local accountant associations. Their training methods all adopt an apprenticeship system. Those who aspire to become accountants must, after graduating from secondary school, first take a preliminary examination administered by the accountant association. After passing the examination and being admitted, they become apprentices to an accountant. During the apprenticeship, they not only do not receive any salary, but also have to pay considerable fees. The apprenticeship period is five years, but after two and a half years, they must pass an intermediate examination. After passing, they continue their apprenticeship. After five years, they must still pass an examination. After passing the examination, they can join the association and be called an "Associate." Among the above qualifications, those who have graduated from a university can be exempted from the examination and have their apprenticeship period shortened to three years. However, the so-called "Associate" is only a type of associate membership, so they can only assist accountants and cannot work independently. However, they receive a salary during the assistant period. After five years as an assistant, they can use "Fellow of Chartered Accountant." After continuing to practice for five years, they can be renamed "Member" (the American "Member" is similar to the British "Fellow"). It is clear that there is a difference in strictness.

Among all the countries in the world that restrict accountant qualifications, Britain should be considered the best, followed by the United States. In other countries, such as Germany, examinations must also be taken. However, the accountant examination is administered by the Chamber of Commerce. Those who wish to become accountants, after passing the examination, can take an oath in the Chamber of Commerce and be called sworn accountants. In France, two examinations and five years of practice are also required before being recognized as a public accountant. The regulations are announced by the government. However, in Japan, although all other cultural relics and systems can imitate Europe and the United States and are more developed than our country, the accountant profession is later than China. In Japan, accountants are called "Keirishi." The Keirishi Act was officially promulgated in 1927 (Showa 2), dividing it into examination and review categories. However, because the qualifications for review are too broad, the number of people is very large (reaching more than 7,000 by the end of 1935), and the types of people are extremely mixed, resulting in the social credibility not being as solid as in Britain, Germany, and France. However, due to strong opposition from all parties, the Keirishi Act may also be revised in the near future.

The first promulgation of the Accountant Regulations in our country was in September 1918. At that time, I introduced it in the "Banking Weekly" and commented on the advantages and disadvantages of the system. However, because the qualifications at that time required graduation from a university business school and five years or more as the chief accountant in a bank or company with a capital of more than 500,000 yuan, it was too strict. Therefore, by July 1921, only 13 people had obtained accountant certificates. In July 1923, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, considering that the regulations were too strict and hindered the development of the accountant profession, revised them. Those who had one of the above two qualifications could register as an accountant. After this revision, because the restrictions were suddenly relaxed, dozens of people were added in a few months, most of whom obtained certificates based on experience. Those who graduated from schools also mostly failed to have sufficient study in accounting subjects. Therefore, although the number of people increased temporarily (a total of more than 250 people by 1926), they contributed little to the development of the accountant profession, and the number of those who actually practiced was very small. Until the establishment of the National Government, on the one hand, it was considered that the restrictions on accountant qualifications in the past were too broad and could not be trusted by the society, so the Accountant Registration Regulations were promulgated, adopting strict principles, with examination as the principle and review as the exception. At the same time, because domestic industrial and commercial enterprises gradually showed an active trend, although the accountant laws and regulations were revised twice by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Ministry of Industry, the restrictions on qualifications were still focused on both knowledge and experience, and the number of accountants in the country also increased significantly (statistics showed that it had exceeded 1,400 by the end of 1935). It is a great blessing to see that the accountant profession in our country will have a healthy development.

New Brazilian Minister to China, Mr. Renato Lacerda Lago, Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 89

Former Minister, Mr. Wei Luosu, Arrived Together From Japan

Conversation Revealed that the Situation of Overseas Chinese in Brazil is Very Good

The new Brazilian Minister to China, Mr. Renato Lacerda Lago, arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 1:45 PM aboard the President McKinley of the Dollar Steamship Lines with his wife, a young son, and a maid, to take up his post. The former Brazilian Minister to China, Mr. Wei Luosu, who has been promoted to Ambassador to Japan, also arrived from Japan to welcome his wife. Mr. Lago gave a speech on board the ship to a reporter from the New Sound Press, outlining his aspirations for coming to China. Details are as follows:

Arrival Situation

The ship entered the port at noon yesterday and docked at the Dollar Line pier in Bailianjing, Pudong at 1:45 PM. The Chargé d'Affaires of the Brazilian Embassy, Mr. and Mrs. Barbosa, and the Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Branco, who had rushed over, took the Dollar Line tender to greet him at 1:15 PM. Minister Lago met with the representatives on the ship and talked briefly. He then changed to the tender and landed at the new customs pier at 2:45 PM. Mr. Zhao Tiezhang, Deputy Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of our country, was there to meet him. Minister Lago shook hands with Mr. Zhao and greeted him before driving with his wife to the Cathay Mansions on Route Pottier for a rest.

Brazilian New Minister Mr. Renato Lacerda Lago and his Wife (International Press Photo)

Minister Wei Arrived Together

Besides his wife and son, the former Brazilian Minister to China, now Ambassador to Japan, Mr. Wei Luosu, also arrived with Minister Lago. Mr. Wei was transferred to Japan this autumn. His wife will come from Europe on the German ship, Gneisenau, arriving in Shanghai on the 8th. Therefore, he specially arrived with Minister Lago from Japan yesterday to welcome her. After his wife arrives in Shanghai, he will go to Japan to take up his post. According to Mr. Wei, he is pleased to revisit his old post.

Speech Delivered

Minister Lago gave a speech on board the ship yesterday to a reporter from the New Sound Press, saying: "I am very fortunate to be appointed as the envoy to China. This is my first visit. China is a world-renowned ancient country, which I have always admired. There are quite a few Chinese residing in Brazil, and their various businesses are doing well. The relationship with the people of my country is also harmonious. The relationship between China and Brazil is close. In the future, we should strive to improve it. On my way to China, I passed through Japan, which was purely a transit. I did not meet with any Japanese officials. After arriving in Shanghai, I will rest first. When Chairman Lin schedules a meeting, I will go to Nanjing to meet him and present my credentials before going to Peiping to take up my post."

Mr. Lago's Brief Biography

Mr. Lago is not tall, but very energetic. When he arrived yesterday, he wore a dark blue serge casual suit and a beige straight woolen coat. He is 45 years old and has been serving in the diplomatic field for many years. He has served as the secretary of the Brazilian Embassy in Caracas, Venezuela, and the Brazilian Embassy in Berlin, Germany. Recently, he was transferred from the Director of the Treaty Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to China.

Interest Rate Reduction Measures

After concrete measures are decided, they will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval before implementation. However, the banking and money shop industries agree in principle to reduce interest rates. The prerequisite is to reduce deposit interest rates first, and then reduce loan interest rates. Zhejiang Province Tung Oil Loan Contracted in Shanghai. Total Loan Amount of 30,000 Yuan from the Shanghai Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau

According to the New Sound Press, the loan from the Shanghai Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau to finance tung oil production in Zhejiang Province was formally signed in Shanghai on the 1st of this month by Yu Kexiao, manager of the Zhejiang Jinhua Yong Bank, and Shen Shuyu, manager of the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau. This contract has been sent to Zhejiang and will be signed by the Construction Department, as the Zhejiang Construction Department is the guarantor for this loan. According to Director Zhao of the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau, the total amount of the tung oil production loan is 30,000 yuan, with an annual interest rate of 9%. The loan will be released to tung farmers by local post offices in Zhejiang, with a term of no more than two months. The discount rate for collateral is 60% of the market price, with a maximum of 70%. The tung oil collateral will be stored in warehouses designated by the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau and the Jinhua Yong Bank. Once the Construction Department signs the contract, the loan will be released.

The Central Bank Raised the Exchange Rate for U.S. Dollars 96

30.25 Yuan per Hundred Since the Day Before Yesterday

The Exchange Rate for British Pounds Remains at One Shilling and Two and a Half Pence

According to the China East News Agency, at the end of last month, speculators dumped U.S. dollars, and the Central Bank bought them at a high price of 30 yuan. The price of British pounds remains at one shilling and two and a half pence, making it impossible for speculators to buy shillings and dump dollars. The Ports of Yantai and Weihaiwei Have Been Frozen in Succession, and the Northern Shipping Route is Almost Cut Off 98

The Baihe River in Tianjin was frozen first, and the sea off Dagu Port has been frozen for more than 100 miles since January 15, blocking the entire shipping route. More than a dozen merchant ships have been surrounded by ice. The Tianjin icebreaker has been damaged twice while rescuing the ice-trapped ships. It has been 20 days now, and the ice has not yet thawed. Unexpectedly, the weather has become even colder in recent days, and the freezing range has extended from Dagu and Tianjin to Yantai and Weihaiwei. Yesterday, Shanghai received a telegram stating that the ice outside the port of Yantai is one foot thick, making navigation difficult. The weather in Weihaiwei has also dropped to 10 degrees below freezing, which is unprecedented.

"Gongping" Damaged The "Gongping" ship of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which also serves as a training ship for graduates of the Wusong Merchant Marine School, has a displacement of 2,705 tons, a length of 320 feet, a width of 64 feet, and an engine power of 2,020 horsepower. It was built in 1894. It was originally scheduled to go to Yantai. On the 4th of this month, when it sailed to Zhifu, there was already ice at the mouth of the Yantai Sea. When the ship entered Zhifu, its hull rubbed against the solid ice, causing damage to the iron plates in the bow cabin, which leaked water. The shipowner telegraphed Shanghai to report the situation yesterday. The General Bureau received the news and temporarily ordered the ship to berth in Yantai for repairs.

Exports Also Obstructed Since mid-January, Chinese merchant ships have been blocked by ice and have stopped sailing to North China. Shanghai is crowded with passengers and goods. Therefore, British companies Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire took the opportunity to increase freight rates by 40% and risked sending ships north. At first, they were able to use icebreaking equipment to break through the ice, but in recent days, the cold has intensified, and the ice layer has become thicker. The two seaports of Yantai and Weihaiwei have also been successively frozen, causing Swire's ships, such as "Zhejiang", "Hunan", and "Huizhou", to be blocked in the North China Sea, and Butterfield & Swire's "Busheng" ship has also been frozen. Their "Lisheng" and "Dingsheng" ships have been damaged and are being repaired, resulting in eight or nine out of ten Shanghai-Tianjin liners being suspended. The Northern shipping route is almost completely cut off. Although Swire's ships, such as "Shengjing", "Ganzhou", and "Yuezhou", are still sailing, they must wait for telegrams from Tianjin in Qingdao to determine their course.
