National Federation of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance Requesting Exemption of Porcelain Export Tax 101

Customs' Estimated Taxation of Porcelain Merchants Is Unbearable; Request to Allow Exemption According to Silk and Tea Precedent.

The National Federation of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating, "We have recently received a letter from the Jingdezhen Chamber of Commerce in Jiangxi, which states, 'Respectfully, according to the joint statement of fourteen porcelain firms including Meicheng, Shuntaixiang, Heshenglong, Tianshunxiang, Jiangxi Office Yuexingshang, Yong'an Company, Guangyihe Tongji, Ourui Ji, Wang Qingfeng, Zhan Zhenji, and He Hongji, that the customs' harsh taxation based on the estimated value of porcelain exports is unbearable, and earnestly requests that the Ministry be asked to approve the exemption according to the precedent of tax exemption for silk and tea exports in order to save the porcelain industry. We believe that Jingdezhen porcelain has a long history and is world-renowned. In recent years, it has suffered from natural disasters and banditry internally, and the pressure of foreign porcelain dumping externally. Its total output has decreased from over ten million to three million. In terms of porcelain exports, the number is undoubtedly small. Therefore, the government has reformed export taxes, exempting fine paintings and red flowers, as well as coarse white-bodied blue-and-white porcelain. Unexpectedly, after implementation, overseas trade has declined daily. The reason is that the porcelain recognized by customs as tax-exempt is all painted with foreign pigments, and the quality is too poor to meet Western needs. Merchants have consistently lost money and dare not try again. Currently, Westerners want to buy two types of lamps: lamp bottles and lamp stands, both for installing electric lights, as well as umbrella stands and flower pots and tea sets, all of which are ordinary daily necessities, but they must be painted with Chinese pigments to meet the requirements. However, customs officials in Jiujiang do not recognize the nature of porcelain. Upon seeing the above types of porcelain painted with Chinese pigments, they insist on classifying them as antiques or decorative items, and assess taxes. Porcelain merchants have repeatedly negotiated without success. Everyone knows that domestically produced porcelain is only manufactured by hand and can only deteriorate, not improve. Its models and colors are purely based on common old methods and are not imitation antiques. If the government imposes this small tax, it will affect merchants' operations and workers' unemployment. This is the first point for which exemption should be requested. The above types of porcelain are daily necessities for Westerners, and their value is very low. However, once customs officials misidentify and assess them, excessive taxes must be paid. The customs tax rate is nominally 8.25 yuan per hundred, but in reality, it has been taxed 13.6 yuan to 41.6 yuan, exceeding the original tax rate by almost five times (see the attached comparative table of customs' estimated taxation of porcelain). Not only has this porcelain export not been exempted from tax, but it has been burdened with heavy taxes. This is the second point for which exemption should be requested. The above types of porcelain are also subject to a 70% import tax when shipped abroad. If the Chinese tax bill contains the words 'antiques', the tax rate will be increased again, and no one will care about Chinese porcelain. This is the third point for which exemption should be requested. Therefore, porcelain painted with Chinese pigments is not an imitation of special antiques. If taxed based on the original cost, porcelain merchants are unable to bear it. If no measures are taken to provide relief, porcelain exports will disappear, suppressing domestic porcelain and promoting foreign porcelain. This tariff policy lacks the intention of protection. Furthermore, exports of domestic silk and tea are not only completely tax-exempt but also assisted and encouraged in various ways. Why should porcelain alone be left out? In addition to submitting a request to the Jiangxi Provincial Government and the Porcelain Industry Administration to forward the request, we hereby submit the comparative table of customs' estimated taxation of porcelain and request verification and approval. We earnestly request that you forward the request to the Ministry of Finance to approve the exemption according to the precedent of tax exemption for silk and tea exports in order to save the porcelain industry and relieve merchants' difficulties.' We find that the porcelain merchants are catering to Western needs by using Chinese pigments, but customs considers them as imitation antiques and imposes taxes, which exceed the original tax by four or five times. The merchants are unable to bear this heavy burden. Furthermore, at a time when foreign porcelain is being dumped and domestic porcelain is declining, vigorous protection is necessary to promote development. The request to apply the precedent of tax exemption for silk and tea exports is appropriate, as both are domestic products and should be treated equally. Accordingly, we enclose a comparative table of customs' estimated taxation for your reference. We earnestly request that you approve the submission to the Ministry of Finance for verification and instruction, which will be deeply appreciated.' Therefore, we hereby cable your Ministry for review and approval, earnestly requesting that you approve the precedent of tax exemption for silk and tea exports and instruct all customs offices to comply in order to save domestic porcelain. Attachment: Chairman Lin Kanghou of the National Federation of Commerce."

Domestically Produced Cigarette Paper Successfully Researched 104

Minfeng Paper Mill Repeatedly Tested; Raising Funds for Production, Goods to Be Shipped in April

Dagon Agency reports: The amount of cigarettes consumed by our people each year is very large, and the cardboard for cigarette boxes and cigarette paper are mostly imported, and the annual loss is alarming. Now the Minfeng Paper Manufacturing Company in this city has researched and manufactured cigarette paper. In addition to making cardboard for cigarette boxes, it has recently imitated the outer wrapping paper of cigarettes and has been successful. It is expected that the goods can be shipped in April of this year. If it can replace foreign goods in the future, it can reduce leakage of four or five million yuan each year. The Dagon Agency reporter visited Jin Runxiang, the person in charge of the company, yesterday to ask about the imitation process. The details are recorded as follows:

Cigarette Paper Is Difficult to Manufacture: The white paper on the outside of the cigarette, which smokers usually do not pay much attention to, is quite difficult to manufacture because ordinary paper has an odor when burned that is difficult for people to smell. If it is used to wrap cigarettes, there will be an unbearable paper smell when smoking. At the same time, the paper often has small holes. If it is used to wrap cigarettes, it cannot be smoked because of air leakage. Furthermore, the burning speed must be equal to the speed of the tobacco leaves. If the tobacco leaves have burned out but the paper has not yet burned out, it will be hollow. Or if the paper has burned out but the tobacco leaves have not yet burned out, the tobacco leaves will be scattered and cannot be smoked again. Therefore, the manufacture of this kind of surface paper must have three conditions: Paper is pure white and odorless; paper is strong and has no holes; and the burning speed is the same as the burning speed of tobacco leaves. Therefore, it is quite difficult to manufacture.

Three Years of Research to Achieve Success: The Minfeng factory has been researching and manufacturing cigarette wrapping paper for two or three years, and has conducted several tests and discussions with painstaking effort. As a result, it found considerable plant raw materials and water volume, and three years ago sent engineer Chen to Germany with this water and raw materials for testing. It was again sent to Japan by two engineers, Chu and Wu, last year for on-the-spot investigation. After returning to China, it was successful after several studies.

Raising Funds for Production, Goods to Be Shipped in April: The factory has now raised 800,000 yuan and ordered two machines from foreign countries specifically for making cigarette paper. One has already been shipped and is currently in production. It is expected that the goods can be shipped in April of this year. It is said that the manufacture of this kind of cigarette surface paper lacks certainty and is extremely risky. At that time, whether it can be completely successful and the same as imported products is still unpredictable, but the company is carefully studying and striving to improve, and it will definitely succeed one day.

Annual Savings of Approximately Five Million: Although cigarette paper is a small item, because there are so many cigarette smokers in the country, its consumption is quite high. The annual output of Chinese cigarette manufacturers reaches seven or eight hundred thousand boxes. Each box requires a roll of cigarette paper, so the annual consumption of cigarette paper is also seven or eight hundred thousand rolls. At the current market price of five or six yuan per roll, the annual cost is four or five million yuan. If the factory can succeed, it can reduce a leakage scar, because the factory's products can be enough for the national Chinese tobacco factory.

We respectfully request that the Ministry of Finance be compassionate and temporarily

Maintain the Original Content in order to Sustain Business and Secure the Livelihood of All Workers: "On January 23 of this year, we received approval from the Ministry of Finance, Qian Zi No. 8434, and various details (original text and table omitted) were also opened later, including the above six kinds of alloy materials. In addition to distributing it, you should also be notified. Although all the fellow traders under the association are in a state of panic, they still deeply feel the sincerity in taking care of the business. However, all the workers under the association have adhered to established methods for hundreds of years, with masters and apprentices passing on knowledge. They have studied it since childhood and used it when they grow up. Families of eight depend on it for a living. Reading the instructions, this alloy material is hard, and it is already in the knowledge of the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, I did not hesitate to give detailed instructions. That is, 'But after heating, you will not feel any difficulties.' I would like to ask the Finance Department to elaborate on the difference between the high and low heat of handicrafts and machine crafts. According to

Scientific Chemical Raw Materials, strong boilers are used, or even oxygen is used. Dong is used for manufacturing. Raw materials are re-applied with pressure, so the color can be kept bright. As for the work of the various industries under the association, the lamp fire tubes are purely hand-hammered to become a chisel. If the raw material ingredients are hard, not only are the lamp fire tubes not enough to melt, but frequent hammering will inevitably cause peeling and unbearable. In addition, workers have shallow knowledge, how can they be said to be scientifically combined? Therefore, the difficulty and simplicity of machine craftsmanship are difficult to force to be the same. There are great difficulties in the raw material color and manual manufacturing. I have to appeal to the Ministry of Finance to grant relief. One also. The Ministry of Finance promulgated measures for exchanging legal tender on November 4 last year. There is a clear distinction between currency and goods. For currency, it is absolutely collected for national treasury management. As for silver products, which are regarded as goods, there is never permission to save. In short, the intention is to plan and take care of the people. My country has been following the trend of learning for thousands of years. Since the Han Dynasty, platinum has been valued, and business stores value reputation. All the colleagues under the association who are familiar to the population have a history of hundreds of years. The silver utensils and ornaments produced by them have always been popular with people in the society. The main purpose of the silver management rules is nothing more than

Prevent the Escape of Silver. The prices of finished products produced by all the industries under the Association are completely different from the price of silver. Each tael has to increase the wages of several yuan, and it is absolutely impossible to use it for transportation and profiteering. I have already stated in detail in the previous presentation. As for mixed gold raw materials, there are currently shops on the market that specialize in producing gold-plated and silver-plated products. However, the result is that most people in the society have abandoned them, and there are often cases of bankruptcy due to failure to support business. From this, it can be seen that although chemical composition can be specified on raw materials, it is feared that the trend of the people's hearts in the society will not be easily changed for a while. All the colleagues under the association and the workers of silverware in the country, or are related to business, or live by working. The actual number of millions of industrial and commercial lives depends on it. This is the second thing that we must request to be given relief to social psychology and the livelihood of employees. What's more, all silver handicrafts are not subject to leakage to the outside world, and are welcomed by the majority of noble people in the country, and are mostly treated as art and treasured. If gold and silver utensils are inevitable to be extravagant, then 30% also contains 30% of pure silver. Even if the color is slightly higher, such as the old 88, in a broad sense, it is equal to 50 steps and 100 steps. Therefore, improving the color and maintaining commerce is truly beneficial to people's livelihood and does not harm the national economy. For chemical alloy raw materials, if they can be used reluctantly in handicraft production, how dare they violate it again and again? Based on the above-mentioned difficulties, I have no choice but to re-present my words in detail. I respectfully request that the Ministry of Finance think about the livelihood of the entire silver shop industry and give extra compassion. Allow the old composition to remain as it is for the time being, maintain the status quo, or come up with a foolproof plan, indicate a way out for survival, so as to protect business and the livelihood of workers. I am so grateful to be waiting for orders. The presenter, Chuan Shengmao, Chairman of the Shanghai Silverware Industry Association."

Tea Inspection Standards Meeting 108

The Shanghai and Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureaus of the Ministry of Industry, for tea inspection, usually formulate various inspection methods each year before the new tea is launched on the market, based on the situation of the previous year, in order to eliminate the export of inferior tea and improve the reputation of foreign trade. This year's inspection standards meeting began on the 30th of last month. Technician Dai Xiaozhou was sent from Hankou to Shanghai to conduct long-term discussions with the tea inspection personnel of the Shanghai Bureau. It is heard that in addition to the detailed regulations on the various standards for export tea and the methods for eliminating colored green tea, starting from this year, it is also planned to add a tea box elimination method. The general regulations stipulate that each tea box must be nailed with twelve corner braces, and the lead foil inside the box should be pasted with strong and clean paper, so that the tea leaves do not come into contact with the lead quality. The weight, origin, and harvesting and manufacturing time must be indicated on the outside of the box for identification. Because the board material of my country's export tea boxes is too thin, many of them are damaged when shipped abroad, and the loss is not worth it. Tea merchants from various countries have also sent letters requesting improvement. In addition to the above regulations, the two bureaus are still jointly discussing various inspection methods in order to unify inspection technology, so that the inspection results of the two bureaus are precise.

Poor Quality of Chinese Silk: Foreign Merchants Export Council Advises Improvement 110

Current Sales Are Very Sluggish, and Merchants from Various States Are Waiting and Watching; New Machinery of the United Silk Mill Has Achieved Results

Huadong News Agency reports: Recently, the Foreign Merchants Association, which distributes and exports Chinese silk in China, has expressed a very bad impression on foreign merchants due to the inferior quality of goods shipped to France and the United States last year. Therefore, they are advising improvement in a friendly manner. Recently, foreign sales have suddenly become silent, which is also said to be the reason. The Huashu News Agency reporter explored the details as a decision.

Poor Quality Affects Reputation: My country's raw silk is the only major bulk export of local products. In recent years, the price of silk abroad has been declining, so that it is no longer as prosperous as in previous years. Last year, the European and American merchants broke through five years of activity, and profit-seeking merchants took advantage of this opportunity to mix inferior goods and pretend to transport them, which has a huge impact on the future of international commerce.

Foreign Chamber of Commerce Makes Recommendations: The Foreign Silk Export Chamber of Commerce organized by French and American merchants in this city made a recommendation in a friendly capacity, hoping that Chinese merchants would make improvements in order to maintain their past reputation. Our belief is that silk industries in various European and American countries will stagnate this year. According to a reporter from the Huashu News Agency, the recommendation was made in a personal capacity, in terms of quality, in terms of quantity, and in terms of unifying the silk reeling vehicles. It also made a contribution.

United Silk Mill Has Achieved Good Results: As for the United Silk Mill formed by the National Economic Commission's Silkworm Guidance Association and various factories, the foreign merchants are very satisfied with the raw silk produced after purchasing 500 new global brand silk cars, and the results are remarkable. It is heard that people in the silk industry say that the loss of changing the old silk car to a five-eyed foreign car is very small. Therefore, the authorities of various silk factories in this city have suggested improvements to the factory owners who rent them in order to restore their reputation.

Sixth Group Wedding Held at City Hall Yesterday; Social Affairs Bureau Presented Commemorative Badges to Guests; Improved Order but Marred by Rain 111

The sixth group wedding of this city was held at 3 p.m. yesterday in the City Hall auditorium. Of the 81, 88, and 93 couples, three were unable to attend due to illness, so the actual number of participating new couples was 94. Director Wu Xingya of the Social Affairs Bureau, the officiant, was in Beijing on official business, so Mayor Wu and Zhang Binghui, the fourth section chief of the bureau, officiated. The auditorium arrangement and the order during the ceremony were more advanced than in previous years. Unfortunately, the weather was uncooperative during the ceremony, with heavy rain pouring down, preventing the audience from standing in the square. The new couples also did not follow the usual practice of walking around in front of the City Hall and were not photographed, which detracted from the grandeur. The Social Affairs Bureau, to preserve a permanent record of the event, distributed copper commemorative badges to the guests and new couples, and gold-plated marriage certificates to the newlyweds. The reporter from New Sound News has investigated and recorded the details as follows:

Auditorium Arrangement More Luxurious Than Before 112

The auditorium arrangement yesterday was more luxurious and magnificent than during the rehearsal the day before, and more perfect compared to previous years. The altar was decorated with various festive ribbons, making it beautiful and dazzling. In front of the altar was a pair of large candlesticks, each with a dragon and phoenix candle. Beside the large candles were five pairs of small candles. Red silk celebratory banners hung on both walls, and a red carpet was laid from the altar to the entrance. Eight pieces of bird and animal Xiang embroidery hung on both walls of the auditorium. The master of ceremonies' seat was in the upper right corner of the altar, the officiant's seat in the center, and the National Academy of Music orchestra's seating was on the right side of the hall. The Public Security Bureau's brass band was seated on the stone steps in front of the main entrance. Shen Zuhui was the master of ceremonies, and Lin Guifu, Lei Kenan, and Tan Jiqing were the auditorium staff.

Candlelight Reflecting, Jointly Forging Good Fortune 113

At 3:25 p.m., with red candles burning brightly and music playing melodiously, the 94 new couples, who had finished dressing in the newlyweds' rest room below the auditorium, were ready. Among them, 81, 88, and 93 couples could not attend due to illness. When the wedding began, Sun Yongyi, Yan Wenkai, and eighteen students from Wan Zhu Elementary School led the way with harmony platters, incense stands, and palace lanterns, guiding the new couples into the auditorium for the ceremony. Director Wu of the Social Affairs Bureau was in Beijing on official business, so Chief Zhang Binghui of the fourth section represented him. First, the newlyweds stood at attention. Second, they paid their respects to the party, national flag, and Sun Yat-sen’s portrait. Third, the representative of the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau read the marriage certificate. Fourth, the new couples faced each other to perform the ceremony. Fifth, the officiant issued marriage certificates and souvenirs to the newlyweds. After each pair of newlyweds went on stage to receive them, they held hands and returned to their seats. Sixth, Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech. Seventh, the new couples bowed to thank the officiant, and the ceremony was completed.

Presented Commemorative Badges, No Photos Due to Rain 114

The etiquette and order of this year's group wedding reached a state of perfection. Not only was the auditorium arrangement luxurious and magnificent, but the order in the auditorium during the ceremony was also more orderly than in previous years. The new couples all wore the prescribed formal attire: blue robes and black jackets for the grooms, white socks, and black satin shoes with white cloth soles; plain satin cheongsams, white veils, white gloves, and shoes and socks of the same color as the formal attire for the brides, holding bouquets. No one did not wear the prescribed shoes and socks, so it was extremely neat and uniform. Yesterday, the new couples were arranged to walk slowly to the auditorium from the City Hall rest room, men on the right and women on the left, along the stepped bridge. After the ceremony, when they stepped out of the auditorium, the rain poured down even more heavily, so they still changed their route, bypassing the City Hall bridge and steps, with men and women separated, women on the left and men on the right, and entered the rest room through the back door to remove their formal attire. Because of the heavy rain, and because photos had been taken the day before, the originally planned photo session of the officiant and newlyweds on the road in front was cancelled. Only firecrackers were set off next to the City Hall road to celebrate. Also, because of the rain during the ceremony, the audience in the square in front of and behind the City Hall were temporarily allowed to enter the auditorium to watch the ceremony without tickets, so the auditorium was extremely crowded yesterday, with about two thousand people, but the order was not disturbed, which was a good phenomenon. The Social Affairs Bureau specially made gold-plated marriage certificate badges and enamel commemorative badges for the newlyweds and guests as keepsakes.

Next Registration Starts on the 10th 115

The City Government's group wedding initiative is to eliminate extravagant wedding customs and promote thrift. Therefore, the ceremonies are broadcast by the city's radio station to both Chinese and foreign audiences. This year's event was also broadcast by the station, with clear sound. Everything in the auditorium, even if not attended in person, was clearly visible through the station's broadcast, benefiting many. The frequency is 900. In addition, holding lavish banquets at the wedding is inconsistent with the purpose of participating in a group wedding. Therefore, all newlyweds were notified to make every effort to practice thrift and eliminate old habits. After the ceremony, according to the person in charge of the Social Affairs Bureau speaking to reporters, this year, the bureau attached great importance to this point, so the results were quite significant. The survey results showed that those who extravagantly held lavish banquets were greatly reduced, which was an improvement compared to the previous year and the first, second, third, and fourth years, and was quite satisfactory. Also, after this year's wedding, registration for the seventh group wedding will begin on the 10th of this month (next Monday) and will end at the end of this month. After investigation, the names of the newlyweds will be announced on March 10, and the wedding ceremony will be held at 3 p.m. on April 1.

Poisoning Case in Courthouse Guard Barracks; Friend Attempted Suicide Due to Unemployment 116

Lu Jianping, a local young man, originally named Lu Yong, whose father ran a milk shop business, joined the Shanghai Volunteer Corps to fight during the January 28th Incident. After the war ended and the Volunteer Corps was disbanded, Lu was also unemployed. Through the introduction of a cousin surnamed Feng, he was recommended to work in a court in this city as a guard squad patrolman. It has been almost two years. Lu is honest and kind, gets along well with his colleagues, and values friendship. A man surnamed Jia, formerly a company commander in the Volunteer Corps, was an old colleague of Lu's and they were close friends. Recently, Jia was unemployed, wandered to Shanghai, and had nowhere to live, so he went to find Lu. Lu, considering Jia a good friend, could not bear to see Jia's hardship on his journey, so he provided Jia with food during the day and allowed Jia to sleep in the courthouse guard barracks at night. The two slept in the same bed. Unexpectedly, Jia, recently unable to find work, had the idea of suicide. On the afternoon of the 4th, while sleeping in the courthouse guard quarters, he took advantage of Lu's absence to drink a bottle of industrial alcohol to kill himself. After drinking it, he lay on Lu's bed, waiting for death to arrive. At about 3 p.m., the poison took effect and he groaned. Lu's colleague Le Quan entered the quarters and discovered him, lifted the quilt, and saw Jia's nose bleeding non-stop, which greatly alarmed him. He immediately reported to squad leader Shen Bingjun, who reported to the general affairs section for investigation. Lu happened to be returning to the courthouse from outside to take over his shift. He immediately helped Jia out and sent him to Guangci Hospital for treatment, hoping to conceal the matter and avoid disputes. However, after Jia entered the hospital, the doctor learned that he had attempted suicide by drinking industrial alcohol, and because it occurred in the courthouse, it was reported to the police station for investigation as a matter of course. After receiving the report, the police station called the court president to investigate. The president learned that Lu had violated court regulations by allowing an outsider to sleep in the barracks, causing a major disaster, and was furious. He ordered Lu to be dismissed from his position and recorded a major demerit against the squad leader for concealing the matter beforehand as a warning. He also instructed the court staff not to allow outsiders to sleep in the barracks in the future. It is said that Jia entered the hospital and, after being given an enema and rescue by the doctor, his life is expected to be saved and he can leave the hospital after a few days of recuperation.

Rui Jingxian Returns from Studying Abroad, Suddenly Quarrels with His Wife; Wife Asks for Mediation to Live Together 117

Rui Jingxian, a young man (around 20 years old, origin unknown) residing at No. 404, Yixia Village, Julida Road, French Concession, married Wang Cuie (around Rui's age, origin unknown) through his parents' arrangement and a matchmaker's words. It has been seven years since then. At the beginning of their marriage, they were inseparable. Two years after their marriage, Rui went abroad in the summer of the 19th year to study in France. After five years of study, he returned to Shanghai last autumn, and the love between the couple suddenly broke down, and quarrels arose. On January 1st of this year, the couple quarreled again over trivial matters, and soon a fight broke out. Rui Wang Cuie left home and returned to Ningbo. Later, she hired a lawyer to send a letter to Rui to negotiate, and published a warning in the newspaper on January 13, demanding that Rui apologize, repent, and live together. After reading the newspaper, Rui Jingxian also hired a lawyer to publish a rebuttal in the newspaper and sent a letter to his father-in-law, Wang Lanfu. Recently, Rui Wang Cuie, unsure of her husband's whereabouts, hired a lawyer to file a petition with the Second Special Court's Civil Division, requesting that Rui Jingxian be summoned to court to mediate living together. The court approved the request. Yesterday, Judge Guo Huaipu summoned both parties to mediate in Civil Court 4. The petitioner Rui Wang Cuie arrived with her lawyer, stating the previous situation, claiming that her husband had changed his attitude a few months after their marriage. After returning from studying abroad, he actually asked her for a divorce. Because she did not agree, he resorted to violence and left home to deal with her passively. On January 1st, he suddenly returned, and when asked where he had been, he shouted that he was not her husband, knocked her to the ground, and kicked her. Because she could no longer endure it, she asked a lawyer to negotiate. Now she is requesting mediation to live together, but her husband is not at home and she does not know where he has gone. As long as she knows where he is, she can go to live with him, etc. The respondent, Rui Jingxian, hired a lawyer to attend on his behalf, claiming that the respondent has always treated the petitioner with respect, and what the petitioner claimed is not true. What was reported in the newspaper was intentionally damaging the respondent's reputation. The respondent has always been at home. The petitioner's lawyer claimed that the respondent was indeed not at home and requested that both parties be summoned to court to meet in person, which would dispel opinions and implement living together. The court verified the statements and advised both parties. Because the opinions of the two parties differed, it was announced that the mediation was unsuccessful and the petitioner was instructed to formally file a lawsuit according to law. They then left the court.

A Murdered Male Corpse Found in Lujiawan, Longhua Road; Head, Face, Abdomen, and Legs All Severely Injured; Seemed to Have Been Doused with Nitric Acid and Then Moved 118

A male corpse was found yesterday morning in Lujiawan, Longhua Road, Shanghai West, covered with a cotton quilt, which seemed suspicious. After being spotted, the relevant police station was notified and dispatched police to find the corpse, which was about 30 years old. The upper body was only wearing a tattered short dark blue wool coat, with the buttons not fastened, exposing the chest and abdomen. The lower body was wearing black cotton trousers and velvet shoes, without socks. The hands were tied with hemp rope across the chest. The head, face, abdomen, and legs were all torn open, covered in blood, and the situation was extremely tragic. It appeared that he had been murdered by being doused with nitric acid and then moved there. Fire in Wangzhi Road Yesterday Morning; Yichang Tobacco Shop Burned Down; Fire Started from Welcoming God Incense and Candles, Spreading to Four Houses; Shop Owner with Fire Insurance Taken into Custody for Questioning 120

Hua Dong News Agency reports: Wu Gaofu, a Ningbo native, nearly 40 years old, led his wife and daughters from his hometown to Shanghai to make a living at the age of 22. Due to poor circumstances, he initially only sold newspapers for a living. Five years later, he saved 500 yuan and opened the

Yichang Tobacco Shop at No. 203, Yongji Lane, Wangzhi Road, French Concession. For more than ten years, the business has been quite successful, especially last year, in the midst of the economic downturn, when it made the most profit. Yesterday was the 13th day of the Lunar New Year (commonly known as the Lantern Festival) and also the day of the Beginning of Spring. Therefore, the hostess got up early in the morning and lit incense and candles in the living room at about 9 a.m. to welcome the gods and the arrival of spring. Unexpectedly, when burning silver ingots, she was careless and sparks flew up, resulting in a

Sudden Fire

That quickly spread through the roof and became uncontrollable. Fortunately, French police officer Tao Delin, No. 596, of the Yongji Lane Patrol Police, first noticed it, sounded the alarm, and telegraphed the Songshan Road Fire Brigade for help. Upon receiving the news, the French Police Station immediately sent a large number of police officers to the scene to maintain order. After a while, fire trucks from various sections arrived and extinguished the fire in 40 minutes, at 10:05 a.m. In addition to the complete destruction of the tobacco and paper shop, the fire also spread to four houses, including the front and back buildings, attics, and pavilions, of the tenants Ma Jiu, etc. An old woman, a tenant, escaped from the upstairs with her hair completely burned, but fortunately there were no deaths or injuries. The shop had

Fire Insurance

with the Siming Savings Society, amounting to 2,000 yuan in legal tender. Therefore, when the fire broke out, a special commissioner from the society went to the scene to investigate. Neighboring shops such as Zhenji, Yongda, and Nanhua Goods Shop were also closed for precaution. The French Police Station then took the fire starter, Wu Zhifu, into custody for questioning about the cause of the fire.

Central News Agency reports: The Municipal Government and the Public Security Bureau of this city have recently paid close attention to fire prevention and public safety in the city. The original text reads: "In accordance with instruction No. 16485 of the Municipal Government, and also based on the factory's report that it will publicly test the fire extinguisher at the Ximen Public Sports Field on January 17 and requested that personnel be sent to attend and monitor, etc., personnel were sent to attend. According to the report (omitted), the powder is pink and its composition is mostly carbon dioxide. It is very effective in extinguishing gasoline and kerosene, but it is not easy to concentrate the powder on the target, which is a disadvantage, etc. After investigation, the fire extinguisher has been proven to be quite effective and will be beneficial to the general public in terms of fire prevention equipment. Therefore, it should be promoted. In addition to reporting the monitoring situation of the test to the Municipal Government and issuing separate orders, it is hereby ordered that you follow these instructions and promote it to your subordinates. This order is from Director Cai Jingjun." Industrial Bureau's Official Vehicle Causes Accident; City Federation Requests Severe Punishment of Driver and Compensation for Victim Jiang Fan 126

The First Special District Citizens' Federation sent a letter to the Industrial Bureau of the Public Concession yesterday, which read: "To whom it may concern: According to a letter from the 35th District Branch of this Federation, member Jiang Xinmin reported that his mother, Jiang Fan, 53 years old, residing at No. 222, Guangxi Road, north of Fuzhou Road, was returning home from shopping at the Zhejiang Road vegetable market at 9:20 a.m. on January 10. While walking past the door of the Fuchang Shoe Store at No. 190, Guangxi Road, a vehicle No. 16251 of the Industrial Bureau suddenly sped up from behind without honking the horn, causing Fan to be unable to avoid it and being knocked down by the vehicle, breaking her left ankle. She fainted on the spot. The driver did not care at all and sped away. After careful investigation at the scene of the accident, it was learned that the vehicle was traveling from south to north. According to traffic regulations, it should have been traveling on the left side. The location where Fan was hit was at the door of the Fuchang Shoe Store at No. 190, east of the road, indicating that the vehicle did not comply with traffic regulations and did not honk the horn in a narrow street, driving at high speed, resulting in an accident, which is a violation of the criminal law of negligence of duty. We request that you uphold justice and request that the Federation negotiate on our behalf. We have learned that your Bureau has strict regulations for vehicles operating within the Concession. Now, the driver of the official vehicle has violated the regulations, disregarding human life and treating it as a trifle, which is very wrong. We are writing to request that your Bureau conduct a thorough investigation of the truth as soon as possible, severely punish the driver who caused the accident to serve as a warning to others, and compensate Jiang Fan, the victim, for all losses in order to clarify responsibility. This is our letter, hoping that you will investigate and handle it accordingly. We would be grateful for your convenience."

Bai Yushuang Pail Throwing Case Concludes Bai Withdraws Lawsuit Two Defendants Sentenced for Disorderly Conduct 128

Bai Yushuang, a Tianjin native residing at No. 7, Bottom of Beile Road, Samsungfang, in the French Concession, currently performing Beng Beng Opera at the Empire Theatre, was attacked with feces thrown by a rogue young fellow countryman Zhao Yuqing on the afternoon of the 27th of last month at 8 PM as she was leaving Samsungfang to go to the Empire Theatre to perform. The feces covered her head and face, and her gray coat, valued at four hundred yuan, was soaked in fecal matter. She cried out loudly, and her mother, neighbors, and detectives chased Zhao to Xujiahui Road, where he was apprehended. His accomplice, Zhang Furui (35 years old, Tianjin native, carpet weaver, residing at No. 15, Xingshunli, Dapu Road, Chinese Territory), Zhao's cousin, was also apprehended and handed over to the Special Second Court for interrogation and investigation. Bai appointed Wu Zhengxu as her lawyer to file a private lawsuit, seeking compensation for the loss of the coat. This has been reported previously. It is now known that the private lawsuit part of the case has been mediated, and Bai agreed to drop it. The public lawsuit part is still being prosecuted by the police according to law. Yesterday was the date for the continued hearing. Bai, as the plaintiff and witness, was required to appear in court. At around 9 AM, she arrived at the court with her lawyer, Wu Zhengxu, and waited on the gallery of the eighth criminal court. Because Bai's artistry is famous throughout Shanghai, male and female court staff rushed to the eighth court to admire Bai's demeanor, causing the court to be crowded with people and almost impossible to move. Bai seemed shy and tucked her face into the fur collar of her brand new gray coat. Judge Sun Pengxian ascended the bench at this time. After hearing several theft cases, he heard this case at 10:30 AM. Bailiffs brought the two defendants, Zhao and Zhang, to the dock. Bai was also summoned to the court. After questioning the defendants about their age and origin, Yuan Jiahan, a lawyer from the police department, stated the facts of the case and prosecuted the defendants Zhao and Zhang for damaging property under Article 354 of the Criminal Law and for violating the police regulations under Article 50, paragraph 1. The judge then questioned the plaintiff Bai Yushuang, who stated that her original name was Li Guiqin, 24 years old, from Tianjin. He asked, "Did these two defendants throw feces on your body?" Bai nodded and replied, "Yes." He asked, "Do you still want to sue them now?" Bai replied, "I don't know them, and I don't have any grudges. What would I sue them for?" He asked, "So you're not suing them, is that right?" She replied, "Yes." The judge turned to Zhao and asked, "Who told you to throw the feces?" The second defendant, Zhang Furui, said, "It was Xu Kaiyuan, who is on the run." The judge asked Zhao whether he was instructed by Zhang Furui. Zhao replied, "Zhang invited me to Xu Kaiyuan's house. I don't know anything else." The judge asked Zhang Furui, "Did you tell the police that the Hebei Native Place Association asked Bai Yushuang to perform, but she refused, so you went to throw feces?" He replied, "I don't know." At this point, the judge asked the police lawyer for his opinion on the case. Lawyer Yuan immediately said, "Article 354 of the Criminal Law is a crime that requires a complaint, and it can be withdrawn according to law. Since the plaintiff is unwilling to pursue the matter, the police department does not object. However, for the violation of police regulations, please make a judgment according to law." The judge then announced the conclusion of the trial and sentenced Zhao Yuqing to ten days of detention for defiling a person's body and Zhang Furui to fifteen days of detention for instigating the defilement of a person's body. The damage to property charge was dismissed. The two defendants immediately declared that they accepted the judgment and were taken away by the bailiffs to be sent to the detention center for execution. Bai Yushuang also withdrew, ordering the servant who came with her to wrap the soiled coat that she brought as evidence and leave the court, and return home by car. The sensational fecal throwing case in Shanghai was thus declared over.

Shiyong (Practical) Science Society Jiangwan Factory Opens 131

A group of students who studied in Germany and graduates of Tongji University have raised 100,000 yuan to develop the manufacture of small, practical items. They built a factory on the Sports Association Road in Jiangwan and purchased the latest automatic machinery from Germany. After years of preparation, the factory officially opened yesterday and invited guests from all walks of life to visit. More than 200 guests arrived. Manager Zheng led them to visit the stamping, casting, and assembly departments. Engineer Jia demonstrated the functions of each machine. Engineer Jia is over 70 years old and has extensive experience in stamping and copper smelting. In his youth, he was sent by Li Hongzhang to study at Krupp and other factories in Germany for many years. After the tour, the factory served refreshments. Manager Deng showed the company's self-made Shuangyue insurance door lock. The lock combines the features of both ordinary iron key locks and Yale deadlock, making it suitable for a variety of uses. Although American companies such as Schlage and Yale had previously created various models based on this method, many domestic factories have also imitated them, but they have not been popularized due to their complexity and difficulty in manufacturing. Now, this dual-purpose insurance door lock is the result of two years of effort by the factory's consultant, Mr. Jiang, and Manager Zheng. It is sturdy, durable, safe, convenient, and has simple parts, which reduces costs and allows Chinese people to obtain high-quality products for a small amount of money. The factory is currently producing 100 locks per day, which are exclusively managed by Fengyuan Company at No. 356 Beijing Road in the city. Soon, a large number of trial locks will be sold, costing only 3 yuan each.

Military Cap Production Cooperative Approved by the Ministry of Military Affairs 134

Since the central government advocated cooperative enterprises, various cooperatives such as consumer, marketing, and credit cooperatives have sprung up like mushrooms after rain. However, production cooperatives are rare. It is reported that all members of the first branch of the Shanghai Military Uniform Workers Union, in order to adhere to the central government's intentions and implement the basic work of the Principle of People's Livelihood, and to enhance the welfare of the workers themselves and for the convenience of all circles, have established a military cap production cooperative, which is the first of its kind in Shanghai. Man Commits Suicide by Poisoning in Hongkou New Hotel 142

At around 9 PM on the 3rd of this month, a middle-aged man with a bald head wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants went to the Hongkou New Hotel at No. 11 Xī'ān Road and rented room number 23. He wrote his name as Liang Dade, 40 years old, local, in the registration book. He immediately closed the door and went to bed. Unexpectedly, for some unknown reason, he secretly ingested opium and committed suicide in the room. The next day at 1 PM, the tea waiter Lu Zhigen saw that the guest had not gotten up yet and went to call him. However, he knocked on the door repeatedly without a response. Realizing that something was wrong, he managed to open the door and found the man moaning in bed, his face pale. He immediately reported to the Hongkou police station, which summoned an ambulance to rush him to the Tongren Hospital for treatment, but to no avail. He soon died. Detective Zhang Shoushan went to investigate and found an empty opium box and a little sugar water in a teapot where the deceased was lying. There were no suicide notes or other items. Therefore, the reason for his suicide and whether he had any family members were difficult to determine at the time. The body was taken to the Fielun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, Inspector Song Genshan was dispatched to the morgue by the First Special Court. He determined that the corpse had died from poisoning due to opium ingestion during his lifetime. Since no family members were found, it was decided to hand over the body to the Pushan Villa for burial.

Fire at Wangjiazhai, Pudong 144

Ashes Ignite Straw Losses of Thousands of Gold

At No. 35 Wangjiazhai, north of Hujia Wood Bridge, Tangqiao, Pudong, in the home of Wu Genbao and Wu Quansheng, two local brothers, three south-facing tile-roofed houses caught fire in the hall where straw and wheat were piled up at around 11 PM the night before last. In an instant, thick smoke filled the air, and the flames spread to the houses, breaking through the roof and becoming uncontrollable. The two families of Wu and others were awakened from their sleep and rushed out, unable to rescue all their clothes and belongings. The Tangqiao police station informed various fire brigades to rush to the scene to put out the fire. After about an hour of burning, all three tile-roofed houses were destroyed, causing losses of more than a thousand taels of gold. After the fire was extinguished, the police station ordered the fire victim Wu Genbao to be taken to the station for questioning about the cause of the fire. According to his statement, the ash that was poured out of the stove, because the embers were not extinguished, the sparks were blown onto the dry straw, causing the fire.

Six Robbers Sentenced Separately Song Laisheng Detained for Further Questioning 147

Hongkou police station Huatamu Bao Shuji and detective Jin Guanya arrested six robbers, Cai Akang, Li Binggen, Liu Yuqin, and others, in a house at No. 41 Zhejiang Road on the 11th of last month. It was found that these people had held weapons and formed gangs between July 20th of the previous year and January of this year to rob Wang Tangde at No. 134 Tangshan Road, Tang Xinmin at No. 106 Huishan Road, Jin Chengfang at No. 8 Zhoujiazui Road, Zhuang Xushi (unsuccessful) at No. 24 Huade Road, Wang Chaochen at No. 125 Xinjiangbang Road, Ying Liji at No. 204 Xian Road, and Zhou Rujin at No. 20 Disiwei Road, taking clothing and silver dollars worth over 700 yuan. Kidnapping a Young Woman: An Old Man Discovers and Reports to the Police 148

Wang Xiaomei, the daughter-in-law of Wang Wushun from Yancheng, is sixteen years old and from Shi Ying. She works as a female worker at the Hongbei Dingxin Yarn Factory in Caojiadu, leaving early and returning late, and has always been peaceful. Recently, she was suddenly seduced by Guo Jiujinzi, a male worker from the same factory (22 years old, from Baoying). The girl was young and ignorant and fell into his trap. Yesterday at 6:50 PM, after the factory let out, he used sweet words to coax her, intending to rape and hide her. As they were walking together on the road, Wang Wushun, her father-in-law, happened to see them. After finding out the truth, he grabbed Guo and reported him to the Laobosheng Road police station. After questioning by Inspector Gu Wentao, the case was deemed to involve rape and fraud and has been transferred to the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Illegally Selling Red Pills Results in Punishment 149

Yesterday at noon, Chinese and Western detectives from the Yangshupu Patrol discovered a red pill (opium substitute) selling operation at 593 East Zhaikou, Yinxiang Port. They arrested Xu Jinsheng, a 16-year-old local accomplice; Zhang Zhitian, a consumer from Anhui; Liu Biao; Liu Gengen from Chongming; Wang Chuncheng, a local; and others. They also seized twenty-four red pills and took them to the patrol station for detention. This morning, they were sent to the Special First Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, prosecuted them according to Articles 259 and 262 of the Criminal Law. He presented the evidence and requested an investigation. Xu Jinsheng confessed that he was an orphan and unable to make a living. He was fooled by the wanted Little Chaozhou, who gave him 20 cents for food every day and begged for leniency. Zhang Zhitian and the others gave evasive statements. Judge Xiao Xiefei sentenced Xu Jinsheng to four years in prison and Zhang Zhitian and the other three to one year and six months each. Before execution, they will be sent to a smoking cessation hospital for treatment for up to one month. The evidence was confiscated.

The Happy Family magazine, published by the Happy Family Publishing House at 110 Sichuan Road, 3rd floor, No. 32, has already published its first issue. Inspectors Capture Three Thieves During Pedestrian Check 152

Li Xiaobao, the leader of the detective squad of the Ximen branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, along with Deputy Leader Qian Tianxiong, foremen Li Shoujiang, detectives Chen Mingsheng, Jin Yushan, Lü Qingkang, Zhao Renxin, Liu Wenhui, Gu Junqing, and police officer Zhang Yannon, conducted a pedestrian check in the Nanshi area yesterday at 6:00 PM. At the entrance of the cigarette paper shop at 240 Luban Road and Xuxie Road intersection, they encountered five suspicious individuals and immediately stepped forward to intercept them. They captured three thieves (the other two escaped). One thief, Mao Erlang, 18 years old from Haimen, was found with a large Mauser pistol (serial number 109836) and seven bullets. Another was Zhang Baoqi, 30 years old from Haimen, and the third was Liu Jiangbing, 29 years old from Haimen. All three were taken to the Ximen branch for interrogation. Liu Jiangbing confessed that their accomplice, Lao Chen, lived in a shack on Xihua Road and had two pistols, one of which Mao Erlang had taken. The other was a four-inch pistol located in Rihui Lane on Jin Shenfu Road. After obtaining this information, they immediately went with the Western and Chinese detectives from the French Concession police station to arrest him, but he was not found. At the same time, they arrested another accomplice, Shi Jianglang, 31 years old from Haimen, in Nanshi. Mao Erlang also confessed that they had planned to rob Li Wenbiao at 89 Xingshun Lane, Luban Road, after meeting at the Tiger Stove in Wajia Bay today. After a brief interrogation by Director Yao, they were all sent to the main bureau for further investigation.

Report on January Charitable Activities of the Pushan Villa 153

In January of the 25th year, the Shanghai Pushan Villa collected 134 large coffins and 2,874 small coffins in both the Chinese and foreign concessions. It distributed 1,659 coffins of various sizes, including 27 large coffins and 1,633 small coffins collected by the villa itself. The Xiqiao Nanshi branch and various charitable halls in the French Concession collected 538 small coffins. Various police stations and health departments in the Public Concession sent notices of abandoned infant corpses and unclaimed bodies from autopsy sites and hospitals, collecting 96 large coffins and 685 small coffins. The First Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society collected one large coffin, the Shanghai Plague Hospital collected four large coffins, the Lianyi Charity Association collected two large coffins and 18 small coffins, the Tongren Hospital collected two large coffins, the Zhongde Hospital collected one large coffin, and the Chaozhou Heji Hospital collected one large coffin. All of these bodies were collected by the villa's vehicles and transported to the Yichang Tangqiao cemetery for burial and marked for future identification. Additionally, the Bai Shizi Pushan Maternity Hospital on Xinmin Road in Zhabei provided medical consultations and medicine to a total of 1,783 people.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for yesterday at 4:30 PM stated: Shandong and the surrounding areas will be cloudy and cold with snowfall and strong northwest to northeast winds. The Yangtze River basin and this area will be cloudy and quite cold with rain or snow and strong northeast to northwest winds due to the passage of a low-pressure system moving towards the northeast. The East China Sea will have rain and strong gales. The Taiwan Strait will have strong northeast seasonal winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this area was a maximum of 45.5 and a minimum of 34.7. On the same day last year, the maximum was 53.4 and the minimum was 34.3.

The Cigarette Industry in Shanghai (Continued) 157

Compiled by China Credit Information

(Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview, No. 12)

2. The Status and Actual Situation of the Cigarette Industry in Shanghai

It goes without saying that the cigarette industry in Shanghai occupies an important position in the national industry. However, it is difficult to know the exact percentage it accounts for, as there is currently a lack of national statistics for the industry. For now, let's make a comparison between Shanghai and the four provinces of Zhejiang, Anhui, Hebei, and Shandong to get a glimpse. According to the China Yearbook of 1925, there were a total of 53 cigarette factories in the aforementioned five regions. Shanghai accounted for 44 factories, while the other four regions accounted for only 9 factories. At the same time, the capital of the former totaled 18,992,000 yuan, while the latter totaled only 390,000 yuan. Therefore, it is not an exaggeration to say that without Shanghai, there would be no cigarette industry in China. Now, the names, addresses, etc. of the main cigarette factories in this area (those with capital of more than 100,000 yuan) are listed as follows:

List of Major Chinese-Owned Cigarette Factories in Shanghai

Factory Name Factory Address Year Established Capital (Thousands of Units)

The Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company is an important stronghold of the national cigarette industry, and Huacheng is a rising star in the industry, both occupying very important positions. In addition to the manufacturing plants listed in the previous table, Nanyang also has many general and branch offices in Shanghai, Hong Kong, Hankou, and other ports, with a very large scale. The company was originally unlimited in nature, but was changed to a limited liability company in 1918. Currently, Chen Bingqian is the chairman and Jian Yujie is the general manager. The company has many brands, with White Gold Dragon, Great Wall, and Great Linked Pearls being the most famous. The Huacheng Tobacco Company has a distribution office in Zhongzha Lane, Ningbo Road. It was changed to a joint-stock limited liability company in 1923. The current general manager is Dai Gengxin from Zhenhai. The company has two new manufacturing plants, covering an area of ​​12 mu, with perfect machinery and equipment. Its products are most popular with the Beautiful Golden Mouse brand.

In August of last year, the Huafie Tobacco Company was established with a capital of 500,000 yuan, almost entirely supplied by the Philipine Aromatic Cigarette Manufacture Co. The director and general manager is Lin Zhaopin, who has considerable experience in the cigarette industry. The factory and general office are located on Baoding Road, and the distribution office is located on Niuzhuang Road. The houses are all rented, with a monthly rent of more than 700 yuan. The factory has three cigarette-making machines, two tobacco-cutting machines, one baling machine, and other assets totaling about 200,000 yuan. The products include Hero, White House, and Yellow Girl brands. It is said that the factory's cigarette-making machine can produce 1,200 cigarettes per minute and 800 cigars.

When studying the cigarette industry in China or Shanghai, the most important thing we cannot ignore is the superior position of the British American Tobacco Company. The company was originally named the American-owned Mao Sheng Foreign Company. Later, because the American merchants did not intend to operate it, it was transferred to the Xielong Foreign Company, and then transferred to the Fengyu Foreign Company. In 1903, Fengyu sold it to the London British American Tobacco Company, becoming the company's general company in China. The general office of the British American Tobacco Company in Shanghai is located at 6 Suzhou Road, with branches in important towns throughout the interior. There are its manufacturing plants at Lujiazui and Lujiadu in Pudong, and 67 Jiao, Taopeng Road. Its capital is strong and its equipment is complete, above Nanyang and Huacheng. At the same time, the tobacco leaf market in the area around Lu, Wan, and Yu is entirely controlled by the company. And since November 1, 1934, it has changed its brand name to Yizhong Transport and Sales Tobacco Company to avoid attention and reduce prices for dumping, with a very profound intention. (To be continued)

Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School Establishes a Physical Education Teacher Training Class 161

The Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School in Jiangwan has been committed to cultivating female physical education teachers and has achieved remarkable results. The school has recently realized that physical education is changing with each passing day, theories are emerging, and teaching and learning are both advancing with the times and cannot be confined to old ways. However, female physical education teachers serving in primary and secondary schools in various places often feel a lack of new knowledge and have sent letters to the school to discuss short-term refresher courses. The school, based on the spirit of service, has added a female physical education teacher training class starting this semester, enrolling female physical education teachers who are interested in supplementing their knowledge or women who have graduated from physical education schools and want to enrich their academic service to society. They will be taught the latest theories and techniques of physical education to become complete talents. The training period is half a year, and the time is economical and convenient, and the curriculum is very complete and practical. It is said that simple brochures are printed and will be sent upon request by mail.

After the End of the Student Movement in Beiping: No Problem with the Opening of Schools; Tsinghua and Yanjing Universities Begin Make-Up Classes; Municipal and Private Primary and Secondary Schools Also Have Classes 167

(Beiping News) Since the patriotic student movement in Beiping ended invisibly, it has been more than a month. Schools have been suspended for a long time. Although some students actively carried out rural propaganda, they failed to achieve satisfactory results due to environmental factors. The propaganda team was forced to return to Ping by train. Other students advocated opening schools and classes, and the number of students in favor of going to class gradually increased. Therefore, the Student Union also passed a resolution to resume classes. Therefore, there is no problem with the opening of schools in Beiping. After all universities and elementary schools opened on February 1, Tsinghua and Yanjing Universities started classes yesterday. Peking University is scheduled to start classes on the 6th, and more than 300 people have registered. Beiping University and Normal University are scheduled to start classes on the 8th, and China College is scheduled to start classes on the 12th. Municipal and private primary and secondary schools will officially start classes within two days. The schools have now returned to normal. The Ping City Social Bureau is scheduled to send supervisors to schools at all levels from the 4th to conduct opening inspections, assess the class situation, and the school's order. The Ping City Compulsory Education Committee's various short-term schools have completed their winter vacation and opened on the 31st of last month. On the afternoon of the 3rd, Yuan Zuoxi, chairman of the Standing Committee of the Compulsory Education Association, and Sun Shiqing, a member of the Standing Committee, went to various districts to inspect and checked more than a dozen short-term elementary schools. They studied the situation after the opening in detail. It is said that Yuan and others will continue to set off for inspections in the coming days. In addition, the Rotary Elementary Schools established by the Ministry of Railways in Ping City recently discussed the opening date together at Rotary No. 2 Elementary School and decided to open on February 15 and start classes on the 17th. The schools have notified the parents of the students the other day.

After Yanjing University started its spring semester on February 1, most of the students who returned home for the winter vacation have arrived at the school to register. Starting from the 3rd (Monday), the school has already begun to make up for the courses missed in the previous semester. Except for those who have not returned to school and cannot attend classes, the students in the school are attending classes as usual. Registration for students in the school is scheduled to start on Friday, February 7, and end on Saturday afternoon. Classes will be held as usual during the registration period. Registration for students returning to school for the second semester is scheduled to be held from February 28 to February 29. All those who fail to attend classes during the make-up period must make them up by March 7. Tsinghua University has already had more than 1,020 people register. Those who have not paid the fees will continue to pay the fees today. Starting on the morning of the 4th, students of all levels have been attending classes to make up for the unfinished courses of the previous semester, and the order is very good. (Jin)

This Year's Four Major Centers of Educational Administration in Hubei Province 168

The Hubei Provincial Department of Education has four major centers for its educational administration policy this year (24th year): (1) "Expanding vocational education" with a focus on improving labor education, reorganizing the original vocational education departments, and establishing agricultural schools and vocational supplementary classes. (2) "Promoting popular education" with a focus on establishing compulsory education, promoting vocational protection elementary schools, carrying out literacy campaigns, implementing broadcast education, and increasing public education institutions. (3) "Improving scientific education" with a focus on increasing scientific equipment, reviewing and supplementing scientific teaching guidance, and encouraging scientific research. (4) "Encouraging human education" with a focus on the New Life Movement, military management Boy Scout training, music cultivation, and health activities.

National Law Colleges and Departments Organize: The Establishment of the Chinese Legal Education Association 169

Chairman Yang Yongqing Reports on the Purpose of Establishment

Today's Continued Meeting to Discuss National Crisis Education, etc.

And Invite Guo Yunguan, Zhang Yaozeng, etc. to Give Lectures

The Chinese Legal Education Association was initiated and organized by eighteen colleges and departments across the country based on the resolution of the National Judicial Conference last year. After a long period of preparation, the inaugural meeting and the first annual meeting were held at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge in this city yesterday morning at 9:00 AM. The inaugural ceremony was held in the morning, the association's charter was discussed in the afternoon, and a banquet was held in the evening for Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau, etc. The meeting will continue this morning to discuss important proposals such as national crisis education, and to discuss the date and location of the second annual meeting, and to determine the school in charge for the year. In the afternoon, the President of the First Special District Court, Guo Yunguan, etc., will be invited to give lectures. The details are recorded as follows:

Origin of the Initiative: In May of last year, the Judicial Yuan of the National Government convened the National Judicial Conference in Nanjing. All universities and independent colleges in the country with law departments sent representatives to attend. The attendees included representatives from the Central Political School, Central University, Sun Yat-sen University, Peking University, Peiping University, Guangzhou University, Guangdong National University, Wuhan University, Yenching University, Xiamen University, Great China University, Fudan University, Aurora University, Chaoyang College, Soochow Law School, Shanghai Law School, College of Law and Politics, and Chih Tze College, a total of eighteen schools. Feeling the necessity of an organized group for law departments in the country, they agreed to decide on a simple five-article charter for the Chinese Legal Education Association and decided to convene the first annual meeting in Shanghai during the winter vacation of this semester. Shandong Law School, Fudan University, and Shanghai Law School were entrusted to prepare and notify the other schools. This is the origin of the organization of the association.

Inaugural Meeting: The association held its inaugural meeting and the first annual meeting at the YMCA yesterday morning. Representatives from Fudan University, Soochow Law School, Great China University, Shanghai Law School, College of Law and Politics, China Public School, Peiping Chaoyang College, Xiamen University, Fu! Law School, Aurora University, Chih Tze College, and other ten schools, including Li Denghui, Yang Yongqing, Tong Kai, Shen Junru, Sheng Zhenwei, Zhang Zhirang, Sun Xiaomei, Wang Fuyan, Chen Zhenlu, Huang Puxin, Sun Haoheng, Shan Yudong, Zhou Mei, Zhang Qingzeng, Zhou Xinmin, Xia Anxiu, Wu Jie, and others, attended. Schools that did not send representatives all sent letters entrusting the association to represent them nearby.

Chairman's Address: Yang Yongqing, the president of Soochow University, was elected as the chairman, and Chen Zhenlu of Chaoyang served as the secretary. After the rituals were performed, the chairman stood up and gave an address. In recent years, many academic groups have been established in the country, such as the Science Society of China and the Engineering Society in the field of natural sciences, and the Economics Society and the Political Science Association in the field of social sciences. The gains and losses of legal education are greatly related to the prosperity and decline of the country and the protection of the people. The establishment of this association is extremely necessary and naturally appropriate. The representatives of various schools attending today are mostly legal experts. After the establishment of this association, it will definitely contribute to the improvement of legal education and greatly benefit the future of the rule of law in the country, and so on. Shen Junru then gave a report.

Amendment of the Charter: Following this, the charter was amended. After a long period of discussion, the following was adopted: (1) The association is organized by specialized schools and above in the country with law departments. (2) The purpose of this association is to improve education. (3) This association will hold a meeting once a year, and the location and date will be decided at the previous annual meeting. (4) This association will have each school recommend one to five representatives to attend the meeting. (5) This association will annually elect one to three schools to be in charge of all affairs within the association, which will be determined at each annual meeting. The term will be from August 1st of each year to July 31st of the following year. (6) This charter may be amended at the annual meeting with the consent of more than two-thirds of the schools present.

Banquet for Director Pan: At 7:00 PM in the evening, still at the YMCA, a banquet was held for Director Pan Gongzhan of the Municipal Education Bureau, as well as Guo Yunguan, the president of the First Special District and Second Special District Local Courts of this city, and other chief prosecutors and judges. During the banquet, Shen Junru and Yang Yongqing, among others, gave speeches. Director Pan and the presidents of various courts all gave brief speeches. The gathering ended happily at around 9:00 PM.

Continued Meeting Today: At 9:00 AM this morning, the annual meeting will continue to be held at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge. In addition to discussing important proposals such as whether the department should add academic programs related to law and war to conform to the purpose of national crisis education, the date and location of the second annual meeting will also be decided, as well as various issues such as determining the school in charge for the year. Lectures will be held in the afternoon, with the speakers being Guo Yunguan, the president of the First Special District Court, and Zhang Yaozeng, the former Minister of Justice.

Civic Education Center to Hold the Third Civic Speech Competition 173

Quota of Twenty People, Regardless of Gender, Registration Begins Immediately at the Center

Civic Education Center to Hold the Third Civic Public Speaking Competition 174

The Shanghai Municipal Civic Education Center will continue to hold the third civic speech competition. The quota is set at twenty people, regardless of gender. The competition date is set for 9:00 AM on March 20th at the center. The topic will be chosen by each individual, but should be within the scope of promoting national products. Each speaker will be limited to ten minutes. The judging criteria are: content accounting for 50%, tone accounting for 25%, and posture accounting for 25%. The top five performers with the best scores will be awarded prizes by the center. For registration procedures, please bring your speech manuscript to the second office of the center from today. Those who are admitted will be notified in writing by the center before March 15th and will be issued a competition certificate. Participants must bring their competition certificate with them when competing, otherwise they will be considered to have forfeited their right to participate.
