Shen Bao National Products Special Issue

Industrial Safety 182

— Yang An

With the changing of the year, may you have a smooth passage. In industry and commerce, when we meet, we often extend "Congratulations" and "Good luck" to each other. This is a custom in the business world and is understandable. In my opinion, what the industrial and commercial sectors can congratulate themselves on most is industrial safety; what they can consider most fortunate is also industrial safety. If a factory can operate without disasters and difficulties and pass safely, this is the most congratulatory and fortunate thing. This should be prepared for in peacetime, not just paid attention to on one day. What is prepared? Is the factory building suitable? In case of an emergency, can it be isolated to prevent it from spreading? Is the arrangement of the machines symmetrical? Does the actual work hinder the process? Can dangerous items be avoided? Is the fire protection equipment complete? Is the usual practice skilled? Especially the inspection of steam boilers, the inspection of electrical wires, and places that are easy to catch fire. The goods and items involved should be strictly examined with scientific methods. The ancients said that it is better to move the chimney and remove the firewood than to be burned head and face. Therefore, congratulations and good luck do not need to be shouted, but industrial safety cannot be ignored. The Industrial Health Exhibition organized by the Ministry of Industry and the Central Industrial Inspection Office is set up for this purpose. The leaders of domestic goods factories in Shanghai visited together and gained a lot. Cheng Shoushen of the Shanghai Machinery Association expressed his feelings after the visit: He believed that the safety items listed in the meeting were indispensable equipment for all factories and had great assistance in improving the domestic goods industry. It can be seen that it is valued by the domestic goods industry. I sincerely hope that the leaders of domestic goods factories across the country will unanimously advocate and agree with it, so that this year's trade surplus can be even more amazing.

Impression of Mr. Wang Xiaolai, Enthusiastic about National Products 183

— Zhang Mengzhao

Words that are so wonderful that he advises everyone not to buy things

Mr. Xiaolai has been in Shanghai for 30 years and has spared no effort in serving the community! And with the sound of a large bell, his spirit is a hundred times better? It is especially admirable that he is simple and unadorned, with a spring breeze on his face, so the impression of Mr. is very deep!

I remember that on the opening day of the National Products Exhibition at Penglai Market, Mr. shouted loudly to the crowd! To remind everyone to remember national products and love national products, but the words "Don't buy things" are humorous and contain the amazing words of truth. At that time, the audience was unaware of what was happening. After Mr. explained that "Don't buy Dong× goods, and don't buy Xi× goods," everyone suddenly understood! Usually, "things" are a pronoun for commodities, no wonder the public misunderstood. How can we cut off supplies? I don’t know that Mr.'s speech talent and agile thinking are enough to make people happy. It can also be seen that Mr. is enthusiastic about promoting national products. I don’t have time to visit again, so I’m writing about my previous impressions of Mr. for the people of the country.

Nanjing Central Market Tour 184

— Li Anfu

In this capital, where various enterprises are advancing rapidly, there aren't absolutely no group-style domestic goods markets. The more basic ones include the Xinshi Market at Fuzimiao, while the better ones include the Da Zhonghua Market and the Guohuo Company, etc. However, their inappropriate internal arrangements or lack of goods are clearly insufficient for a metropolis with a population of over a million. Thus, the Nanjing Central Market was born out of the needs of the citizens!

The Central Market is open! Whether to buy things or just to watch the excitement, everyone wants to see this leading market in the capital. So, I also joined the crowd and squeezed in. As soon as I walked onto Zhongzheng Road, the steel-and-concrete archway of the Central Market, resembling a "war victory arch," came into view, especially its towering roof. Walking through the archway, about thirty or forty steps away, is the facade of the Central Market. The grandeur of its architecture and the vastness of its area, in terms of Shanghai, are not inferior to the Continental Market. Moreover, because the roof of the main aisle is made of glass, the quality of light is far beyond what the Continental Market can achieve. At the same time, because No. 1 is the Central Garden, two model gardens were specially built on both sides of the facade, making the facade even more elegant!

Walking through the entrance, you can see shops on both sides. In the middle of the wide corridor, there are also many glass display cases. Some people say this style is like the Dong'an Market in Beiping, but how could the Dong'an Market have such good construction and lighting! Walking through the long corridor and turning to the left, there is another similar long corridor. To put it simply, the design is like a long, narrow 口 (kou) shape with a large 十 (shi) shape in the middle. The downstairs area has the most practical shops, while the upstairs area has restaurants, teahouses, etc. There are a total of 167 shops and stalls, selling products from Beijing, Shanghai, Hankou, Beiping, Fujian, Guangdong, Zhejiang, Sichuan, and other places. It can be said that they are entirely domestic goods. It seems that there is no such large group market in Shanghai, let alone in the capital. At the same time, what is even more satisfying is that there is a management office and regulations, so that all shops can comply with them, such as marking prices, stipulating low-price periods, etc., creating a domestic goods market performing with a new attitude. Moreover, in their plans, there are also amusement parks and cinemas. Undoubtedly, the future of this Central Market will definitely have greater development.

After touring for a week, the reporter feels that we often only shout and do not act in any undertaking. For example, even elementary school students can smoothly chant the slogan of promoting domestic goods, but what has been achieved in that domestic goods year? On various statistical tables of imported goods, the numbers are increasing day by day, while our country, shouting the slogan of promoting domestic goods, is getting poorer day by day. We might as well ask ourselves, what is the reason for this? Isn't it just the effect of knowing only how to shout but not how to do? Therefore, the lesson given to me after seeing the Central Market is that we need a spirit of action.

Hopes for Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year 185

— Shou Qiu

The giant wheel of the times is advancing day by day, and the calendar on the wall is being torn off page by page. In the blink of an eye, this thick calendar has been torn off! Thus, this twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China—the Students' Domestic Goods Year—has also ended! Of course, in this Students' Domestic Goods Year, there have been a few things that are barely satisfactory, but the promotion of domestic goods has not yet succeeded, which is undeniable. Therefore, there is still a need to continue to work hard to promote domestic goods. However, the Student Domestic Goods Year of the 24th year has ended! What year is the 25th year? After several meetings, various groups in Shanghai have designated this year—the 25th year of the Republic of China—as the Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year. According to the word "Citizens," it clearly refers to Shanghai. Therefore, the banner for promoting domestic goods this year is: Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year. We very much agree with this kind of banner. Because Shanghai is the only big city in our country, and Shanghai consumes the most foreign goods. Moreover, Shanghai is also the location of our country's commercial center. Therefore, there are several meanings to using the banner of Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year: First: Since Shanghai is the only big city in our country, Shanghai has the responsibility to lead the whole country; Second: Since Shanghai is the place with the most foreign imports and is also a general transit point for foreign goods, if Shanghai implements the promotion of domestic goods and the use of domestic goods, foreign goods will naturally not come in endlessly! Third: Since Shanghai is the location of the national industrial and commercial center, it is especially appropriate to start with industrial and commercial reforms based on the principle of promoting domestic goods. Therefore, I think the stipulation of Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year is very appropriate. However, as this Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year has just begun, there are a few points that I hope all compatriots across the country will pay attention to:

First: Although this year is Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year, all Chinese people have the obligation to use domestic goods. Do not think that pushing the responsibility onto the people of Shanghai is enough. You must know that the purpose of this year's banner is for the people of Shanghai to lead our national people in using domestic goods. This point must be clearly recognized.

Second: At the beginning of this Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year, everyone can reflect on their own situation in promoting domestic goods last year. If you were able to work hard to implement it, you should work even harder; if you were not able to implement it, you should quickly correct your mistakes.

Third: I hope that all industries and businesses across the country will work hard to improve their products so that every product can meet the needs of the Chinese people, and that the price can be reduced as much as possible within a possible range to achieve cooperation between production, sales, and customers.

Fourth: I hope that all Chinese people will completely use domestic goods from this year onwards.

Finally, I wish the Shanghai Citizens' Use of Domestic Goods Year success!

Finance: Pure Gold Drops; Specie Market Listless 187

Limited Fluctuations in Half a Day; Result is Continued Drop of 2.1 Yuan; Government Bonds Temporarily Settled Today

The gold market yesterday was characterized by a decline in pure gold and continued weakness. However, market sentiment was mediocre, and the price continued to fall by 2.1 yuan. The trend remains uncertain. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw no change in London and a flat market in the US. The forward silver price in Monte Carlo was unchanged, fluctuating by only two or one points. Exchange rates contracted. London raw gold fell five pence. The Central Bank's official rate announcement showed no change in both British and American currencies. The customs gold unit fell eight points. The standard specie price was announced at 1142.5 yuan. Market sentiment was mediocre. In off-exchange trading, the opening price immediately dropped to 44 yuan. Huixiang, Dadecheng and others took advantage of the low price to rise to over 5 yuan. The morning opened with a low price and continued to fall due to multiple sellers. However, buyers maintained at the low price and gradually pulled up the price. The HSBC Bank official rate announcement showed no change in both British and American currencies. After a high, the supply and demand balanced out and hovered around 45 yuan. The silver equalization tax announcement showed a drop of half a point, with insufficient demand. Many parties also emerged. After that, there were still small setbacks. Market sentiment was peaceful, and many took advantage of the low price to maintain their positions. The mid-day trend was still relatively flat and stable. The spot market was strong due to the swap spread. Weight of Cotton Bales Packaging 197

The packaging of cotton in our country has never had a uniform standard, and the decoration varies from place to place. American cotton each bale is 500 pounds, and rolled cotton is 300 pounds. This type of packaging is called the Mei An Yangxing modification method. Indian cotton is 300 pounds per bale, with no difference. The situation of district differences in our country is now recorded. Shaanxi Hua Lingbao Hua generally hits foreign shelves, each piece 500 pounds, totaling 375 Sima scales. There are also large and medium buns. This type of packaging is mostly popular in Shandong, Henan, and other places. Foreign shelves are decorated. The previous weight was 330 jin per bale, and the wooden shelves were earth bundles in the countryside, packed by manpower, with different weights. They are also bundled with hemp rope and lead wire, ranging from 150 jin to 260 jin. The so-called white bag flowers are all made of white cloth running through the bag. Tongzhou flower fire machine flower original flower Taicang flower Wusong flower, etc., stipulate 125 jin per bale, Taicang flower has grass bags, Yao flower is Ningbo flower, 60 jin per bale, and also uses cloth bags. The above jin are all calculated in Sima scales.

Publishing World

The Nature of Nationalism 209

— Ye Qing

National self-awareness is the self-recognition of a nation, and it occurs in oppressed nations. Therefore, the nationalism that awakens national self-awareness is a banner to overthrow imperialism. Hence, its nature is political.

This point is one of the keys to understanding nationalism. Therefore, Zhang Fodai's statement in the Guowen Weekly that "we must put nationalism on a moral foundation to make it a healthy ethical principle that everyone can believe in" (Volume 13, Issue 1) is incorrect.

Then, "the goal of nationalism at this time is nothing more than anti-imperialism, using nationalism to fight against imperialism" (ibid.). Yes, this is precisely the fundamental role of nationalism. It has nothing else beyond this.

Therefore, Zhang Foquan's view that "nationalism is outward-looking, negative, and destructive" (ibid.) is a fundamentally flawed reason for revising nationalism. He does not truly understand nationalism. In fact, are the occurrence, practice, and function of nationalism not all based on the oppressed nation's passive destruction of external aggressive forces to achieve liberation? What nationalism is there besides this?

This does not mean that it has no impact on economic, moral, educational, artistic, and other aspects of life. Of course, it does. The superiority of political life and the interactivity of various aspects of life inevitably extend nationalism to all aspects. Is not the so-called national economy just another name for a national economy?

Similarly, it also has inward-looking, active, and constructive significance. In this respect, is not the anti-imperialist national economy a clear example?

But this never changes the nature of nationalism. On the contrary, its expansion turns economics, morality, education, art, etc., into means of national political movements. In other words, it seeks to create anti-imperialist revolutionary struggles from all aspects.

Then, the inward-looking, active, and constructive nature it expresses in all aspects is merely the activity of the oppressed nation to passively destroy the aggressive forces from outside. Its purpose is to form a revolutionary force independent of imperialism.

If we feel that the work of forming a national revolutionary force is very important, and therefore promote the inward-looking, active, and constructive nature of nationalism, that is to say, we want to advocate national economy, national morality, national education, national art, etc., we may as well regard the inward-looking, active, and constructive nature of nationalism as parallel to the outward-looking, passive, and destructive nature of nationalism.

Then, we can say that nationalism is outward-looking, passive, and destructive with respect to imperialism; and it is inward-looking, active, and constructive with respect to oppressed nations. It is not simple, it contains contradictions, and it is a kind of opposing unity. So be it.

Therefore, Zhang Foquan's view that the inward-looking, active, and constructive nature of nationalism is incompatible with the outward-looking, passive, and destructive nature of nationalism, and his advocacy of using the former to replace the latter, is completely wrong.

Only internal reorganization, not resistance to external insults. Is that not a compromising tendency against overthrowing imperialism?

However, in today's world where imperialist aggression is intensifying, and in today's world where it is extremely necessary to awaken the national self-awareness movement, we must still place special emphasis on the outward-looking, passive, and destructive nature of nationalism. Even when forming a national revolutionary force, that is, when exerting the inward-looking, active, and constructive nature of nationalism, we must also pay attention to this point. Otherwise, it can only create power, not a national revolutionary force, for the purpose of opposing imperialism and achieving national liberation.

Therefore, we cannot but criticize Zhang Foquan's "new interpretation." Everyone in the cultural circles should stand up today to oppose the consciousness of compromise and oppose national abolitionism. Is this not the effort we should make for the most needed national revolutionary movement at present?

Cultural Activities of Chinese Students in Tokyo 210

— Shi Yin

Under sharp surveillance and oppression, thousands of Chinese students remaining in Tokyo have not shown any indication of the increasingly serious national crisis. This cannot but express our dissatisfaction to the students back home who have been sacrificed. However, over the past year, Chinese students in Tokyo have exhibited a good phenomenon that has never been seen in the history of studying in Japan, which is the activity of cultural undertakings. Now we can divide this topic into two points to illustrate:

A Publishing

"Liudong News": This is a small newspaper run by Mr. Chuan Xiangmo, founded in the first half of last year. It was initially a weekly, but later, due to good sales, it was changed to a thrice-weekly. The content in the first few issues was very weak, only introducing some trivial news about the students studying abroad. Later, it gradually introduced important domestic news, so the degree of need for it among students also gradually increased.

"Zawen": It is a periodic small literary publication. At first, many people participated, but later, due to financial difficulties, it could not be maintained, and everyone said goodbye to it, leaving only Bo Sheng, Meng Ke, Ren Baige and others struggling desperately. Although this publication is small, the shadow it has left in the minds of students at home and abroad is very strong. Its attitude is correct, it is active, it is dragging the heavy era forward with a solid hemp rope, and it stands opposite to the reactionary, passive, decadent, and "Analects" that sells laughter to local society. When the fourth issue was released, it was suddenly searched by the Tokyo police and has now been renamed "Zhiwen". It is said that the fifth issue will be released soon.

"Dongliu": Dongliu is also a publication that focuses on literature and art. Although its achievements are not as good as "Zawen," it can also be regarded as a second-rate magazine. If society can allow it to grow well, its future achievements will be considerable. But it suffered the same misfortune as "Zawen". At that time, the editor-in-chief, Mr. Chen, was also taken to the Metropolitan Police Department. Although he was released a long time ago, "Dongliu" has "flowed eastward like water."

"Shige": At first, one sheet was published per issue, which was a periodic publication specializing in poetry. Later, due to poor sales and extreme financial difficulties, everyone left. Finally, Mr. Wei Jin took full responsibility for the economic and editorial aspects and changed it to a magazine, but it only published one issue before passing away.

"Gekijo Geijutsu": A magazine specializing in the study of drama, organized by drama groups remaining in Tokyo. It was recently founded and the content is quite good, but it cannot be published on time due to financial reasons.

"Liudong Gakuho": Edited by Mr. Chen Guting, the content includes politics, economics, literature and art. Three issues have been published. Thanks to Mr. Chen's efforts, it should continue.

"Shakai Chishiki": A comprehensive magazine, divided into international, women's, and literary sections, with an emphasis on the international section. It specializes in introducing international politics, economics, military affairs, diplomacy, and other news to help domestic readers understand the international situation. "Shakai Chishiki" uses extremely economical means and a correct attitude to enable domestic compatriots to find some outlines and routes in this bizarre international political situation. The women's section is run by more than a dozen female students who feel that there are too few women's publications in China. They have specifically allocated a piece of land in "Shakai Chishiki" to say a few words that should be said for women in China. Their purpose is to: study the way out for Chinese women; introduce Japanese women's lives; introduce international women's news; and introduce the lives of Chinese female students studying in Japan. The literary section is responsible for manuscripts and editing by students studying literature and art here. There are no full-length creations, focusing on short works depicting real life and introducing internationally renowned literature and art. Edited by Mr. Zhou Moqiu, the Shanghai Mass Magazine Company is the general distributor, and printing and distribution are also in Shanghai.

"Gakujutsu Kai": A quarterly magazine edited by the Chinese Student Association of Meiji University, edited by Mr. Liu Ji. It was previously suspended due to financial reasons and was only recently published. After it was printed, the Metropolitan Police Department did not allow it to be distributed because there was a blank space inside titled "War and Morality": "Most people in the world hate war. It is immoral to create war against the will of the majority..." Later, following the police's orders, the blank space was deleted before it was allowed to be distributed. The Japanese government must delete this "anti-war" blank space, and we can know their attitude toward peace.

B Drama Graduation

Chinese drama has gained considerable reputation in Tokyo. Everyone only needs to look at the solemn and careful introduction by the famous writer Akita Ujaku in the Asahi Shimbun to know the efforts of Chinese students in drama. There are many drama groups, the main ones being the China Drama Round Table, the China International Drama Association, and the China Student New Drama Association. In terms of performance, the former two are not as good as the latter. The China Student New Drama Association has had several large-scale performances in Tokyo. The "Inspection Commissioner," etc., performed at the Tsukiji Little Theater in November last year, received very good results. Everyone said with certainty that this drama troupe has hope in the future.

In short, Chinese students in Tokyo have absolutely not forgotten the disasters of their motherland. We are always working hard for the motherland, only because the environment is different, the way of working hard is also slightly different, which should be understood by all parties. Teachers here are subjected to inhumane treatment and are under severe surveillance at all times. If it were not for the weakness of the motherland, how could this be? We hope with tears that the motherland can endure hardship and struggle, and hope that the motherland will one day be able to stretch its long-bent waist on the steep and dangerous international terrain!

Bookstore Scenery (Continued) 211

— Li Hengzhi

Another situation that greatly affects pricing is the method of doing "business," such as new bookstores trying to expand their sales network and trying to please bookstore owners in the interior. These bookstore owners know nothing about books, only that the agency discount is large and the commission is high. But if they follow their demands, the new bookstores will inevitably lose money, and the books cannot be sold. Therefore, the smart managers of the new bookstores came up with a way to satisfy both sides, that is, to learn from the foreign goods stores on the road, shouting cheap prices in public, but secretly raising the marked price. As a result, the book industry has not developed in recent years, but the pricing of books has become higher day by day.

As a result, a strange phenomenon has occurred, that is, readers who buy books go to the Shanghai headquarters, and the price is often higher than at the retail outlets in other cities. Books sold at the actual price at the Shanghai headquarters can be purchased at a 30% to 20% discount in other cities. Bookstores in Shanghai that sell other people's books often do not purchase directly from a certain large bookstore nearby, but instead purchase indirectly from retail outlets in other cities, and the price is cheaper than purchasing directly from the headquarters. Retailers do not increase handling fees, etc., but the total price is cheaper than the headquarters, is it not strange? But if we know the above reasons, we will not be surprised. The new bookstore headquarters also wants to lower prices to attract customers, but this conflicts with the interests of the interior retailers. If the headquarters sells at the actual price, and the wholesale price to the industry is 30% off, the interior bookstore owners are satisfied, but if the headquarters also sells at 30% off, and does not give the industry 30% off of 30%, then the agents in various places will return the books. Therefore, smart readers often do not buy books from the headquarters, but turn to the retailers.

After 1929, due to the decline of the cultural movement, the general reading atmosphere declined, and the new book industry has been hit. Since the world economic panic occurred, the purchasing power of readers has become even more exhausted. As a result, the unprecedented tragedy of "half price for all new books" has been forced to occur. This is not good news for readers, but a sign of the bankruptcy of the new book industry. Except for one or two large bookstores that are lining up to prevent others from selling off, most of them are losing money and struggling to survive. Don't you see that many new bookstores that had a history in the past are now in a state of stagnation? Their business has declined, and the expenses are the same. If they do not sell off their inventory as much as possible, they may be forced to close. Since the recent currency reform, the price of paper and other costs have obviously increased a lot. But can you still do as before, because the cost has increased, and then "consult with the industry and add one to the marked price"? The complete collapse of the new book industry is probably in the near future.

As for the "20% off" reprints of books without copyright, although it is a deformed phenomenon and not directly related to the scope of the new book industry, it can also reflect what stage the Chinese publishing and cultural circles have reached today. (To be continued)

Writing and Publishing 212

— Wu Lifu

Mr. Lu Xun recently published an untitled draft in Haiyan, saying that Mr. Zhu Guangqian regarded "serenity" (Serenity) as the extreme realm of poetry, which inevitably narrowed the scope of poetry and "lingered" the poet. Because anyone who sees the overall picture of the poem, or the poet's entire life, as well as the social state acting on the poet, we will naturally abandon any abstract and general statement, such as "pure and peculiar," "elegant," "leisurely," and so on. In fact, we often encounter methods of generalization like Mr. Zhu's in general literary criticism. Like forcibly adding "progressive," "backward," and so on to a certain writer, it is a very obvious example, but because these are newer than "serenity" and "pure and peculiar," many people do not feel how unpleasant they are. In this regard, I can't help but think of the fact that we also have similar vague understandings in the relationship between writing and publishing, which must be pointed out urgently!

Writing is originally about expressing one's feelings directly, without concealing anything, especially without pretense, but when it comes to publishing, it is another matter. In the publications of the past year or two, writers have been restricted by publishing, and they are not allowed to cover up or be ambiguous, making compromises on the one hand and expressing their own meaning on the other. He even uses second-rate things to replace first-class goods, just like a reputable pharmacy replacing first-class goods with second-class goods. If we read this kind of article and think that the writer's original intention is only this, then we are mistaken. One thing that is very clear is: the introduction of Gide-style thinking was particularly popular last year. Gide's treatises, recent actions, speeches, etc. were published in publications. Comparatively speaking, what can show the true face of this cultural figure is the essay describing himself (Translation, Volume 1, Issue 2), the speech titled In Defense of Culture (Current Events, Volume 3, Issue 17), and Gide's life and works (World Literature, Volume 1, Issue 6). What are the things that have been replaced here?

In the third article, we see several major transformations in Gide's life: first, he was a Protestant ascetic, "sleeping on the woodcut at night, jumping into cold water at dawn, and getting up in the middle of the night to pray"; then he thought that "using 'reason' to subdue 'desire' and using 'morality' to destroy 'nature' is 'cruel and unreasonable'," so the dam collapsed, and "he indulged in sensual pleasures"; then, "reason" and "desire" conflicted again, causing him to fall into depression and begin to examine the true meaning of life, finally reaching this conclusion—"If people can regard all actions that do not originate from consciousness as shame, then people's lives can be changed"; therefore, on the one hand, he cursed the greed of capitalism, and on the other hand, he did not negate personal freedom; he finally believed that "individualism in the true sense should be beneficial to society, and it is a mistake to oppose individualism to collective socialism." These few steps depict the process of a large group of modern intellectuals, especially pointing out the "excitement" "lodged in warmth," as distinct from the "sudden rise" "suppressed by long-term physical labor." In the second article, we encounter the few bright and dazzling lines: "I am French, and at the same time an internationalist. I thoroughly approve of scientific socialism, and at the same time I am also a thorough individualist." He obviously wanted to maintain the greatest characteristics of each individual in the new society, and yet he could justify it theoretically. He continued to seek ways to reconcile society and the individual, but the spirit of individualism in capitalist society was still deeply hidden in his personality. Although the proposition he is now singing, "Only when each individual maintains his greatest characteristics can he serve society," can be in line with dialectical interpretation, we always feel that Gide is a little too clever and too skilled in rhetoric. In the first article, he says how much he likes solitude, and even if he wants to express something, he has to choose a relatively indifferent way. Therefore, "What I have chosen is not language, but articles, not news magazines, but single books, not trendy things, but works of art." This makes us understand even more how Gide sympathizes with hermits who "hide their names in famous mountains." Overall, the Gide obtained from these important documents is a type of transformed literati; it is natural to have no great harm to be close to him, however, in terms of the purpose of writing, simply introducing him can only stimulate the general intellectual class to a considerable extent and achieve some wavering effects, but after all, it is not enough to have an active guidance! (To be continued)

Treatment of Neurasthenia 213

— Dr. Feng Shanliang

Neurasthenia often initially occurs as sexual neurasthenia, such as premature ejaculation, nocturnal emission, impotence, etc. Afterward, it gradually progresses to spinal nerve weakness and eventually to cerebral neurasthenia. At this time, symptoms such as dizziness, vertigo, tinnitus, multiple dreams, insomnia, weakness of the limbs, general fatigue, and poor memory occur. In severe cases, pain often occurs in the sacrum. In addition to the patient themselves needing to eliminate the predisposing causes, the lifestyle environment is also very important for treating this condition. For example, work and rest must be moderate, regulate eating times, avoid irregular living, correct thoughts, cut off desires, and choose appropriate nutrients to ensure that the body and mind are quiet and free. Drug treatment is best with endocrine and organic phosphorus, as both are tonics for the nervous system. The human body consumes too much of these two elements, so corresponding supplementation is necessary. However, there are many similar drugs, so it is necessary to pay attention to choosing the best to be effective.

A Survey of Current Smoking Cessation Methods 216

— Dr. She Lei

(1) Gradual Reduction Method, also known as the Substitution Method. This method has been used for a long time. In the past, doctors relied on this method to help people quit smoking. Even though there are many methods for quitting smoking now, this method cannot be completely eliminated. The use of this method involves taking opium substitutes, the best of which are new codeine, gradually reducing the dosage to eliminate the smoking habit.

(2) Blistering Method. This method involves applying blistering agents to the flat areas of the chest, abdomen, and legs of the person quitting. After blisters form, the fluid is extracted and injected back into the body of the person quitting. This method was initially popular in Annam and was invented by Mr. "Madina." The reasoning is that, although the details of this type of blister are not yet fully explained, the positive results obtained in practice are sufficient to prove its effectiveness.

(3) Blood Collection Method. This method involves collecting 5 to 10 cc of blood from the veins of the person quitting. It is then either directly injected back or made into a serum and injected into the muscles of the person quitting. At the same time, glucose is injected to replenish the loss. This method is typically applied seven or eight times to completely eliminate the smoking toxins.

(4) Denaturation Method. This method involves the daily intravenous injection of organic calcium compounds. This gradually separates the smoking toxins combined with cells in the body, eventually leading to their complete disappearance.

(5) Lecithin Method. Lecithin is obtained from animal brain matter, egg yolk, and soybeans. The most effective source is egg yolk. According to users, it rarely produces complete results. Therefore, using it alone is of questionable effectiveness. It can be used to supplement other methods, or other methods can be used to supplement it, to achieve better results.

(6) Sleep Method. Administering large doses of sleeping pills to the person quitting to make them fall asleep and not feel any withdrawal pain, thereby eliminating the smoking habit and achieving the goal of quitting.

— Dr. Liu Xuannü

Gonorrhea is caused by unclean sexual intercourse, which transmits gonococcal diplococci. The most important treatment for gonorrhea is to kill the gonococci to completely eradicate the disease. After gonorrhea is transmitted, gonococci invade various parts of the urethra, with the greatest proliferation and latency in the deep part of the mucosa. If the medicinal power of the drug can deeply penetrate the urethral mucosa and kill all the gonococci, the gonorrhea will be cured. Ringworm and Scabies 219

— Zheng Zhifang

These two are both types of skin diseases. Their cause is due to the parasitic infection of a type of bacteria, causing unbearable itching. Sometimes, it spreads throughout the body, causing even more pain. It often appears and disappears, spreading to each other, making it extremely difficult to eradicate. There are many types of ringworm, such as serpentine ringworm, groin ringworm, and wet ringworm, etc. Regardless of the type of ringworm, it is due to a lack of skin resistance, resulting in bacterial infection. Scabies is divided into dry and wet types, with the wet type being more severe than the dry type, sometimes even with extremely deep sores, and the healing period is longer. Treatment methods, such as mite-killing agents, salicylic acid, zinc oxide, sulfur, etc., are indispensable medications. The recent "Miejue Jun" is made according to this formula, with accurate curative effects, unlike ordinary products. In terms of electrotherapy, mercury quartz lamps and artificial sun lamps all have considerable effects.

Discussion

"Distant Friendship and Close Attack" 222

— Fang

Although there was no so-called diplomacy in ancient China, the practice of persuasion was quite prevalent in various dynasties, especially during the turbulent times when various factions occupied their own territories and declared themselves kings. The so-called "alliance" and "connection" during the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods originated from the mouths of ordinary persuaders. If it weren't for them, perhaps the six kingdoms would not have split apart; if it weren't for them, perhaps the six kingdoms would not have been able to restrain Qin. Su Qin and Zhang Yi both gained high office with a single insightful view. From a modern perspective, this is the diplomatic battle between countries.

"Distant friendship and close attack" was originally the strategy used by the State of Qin during the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods to disperse the power of the six kingdoms in order to gradually annex them. Historically, the use of this diplomatic weapon has been seen in various dynasties, and now the imperialists of our eastern neighbor have actually learned this trick. A Tokyo dispatch from the China United Press on February 1 stated that "Japan's policy towards the world has decided to adopt the principle of 'distant friendship and close attack,' so it will exert its strength against the Soviet Union and China to determine the outcome of life and death; while for the international community, it will express multilateralism, trade, and cooperation..." Looking at this telegram, we can see the clear evidence.

The current era is naturally very different from the Spring and Autumn period. Moreover, the Japanese's so-called "distant friendship and close attack" has a different intention from the Spring and Autumn period. On the one hand, they use the name of anti-Soviet "anti-communism" to appease the opposition of international imperialism, while on the other hand, they plan to "operate step by step" to divide our China. Looking at the current situation in the Northeast, North China, and Inner Mongolia, it is enough to make us feel grief and indignation. Recently, conflicts have occurred frequently between the border of Outer Mongolia, the Soviet Union, and "Manchukuo," even leading to close combat, which shows that the information in this telegram is not without basis. The Japanese use "distant friendship and close attack" and further conclude a "military alliance" with Germany, the vanguard of the West's anti-Soviet movement, which clearly demonstrates their attempt to dominate the Far East and re-divide the world.

Chocolate Girl 223

— Li Yi

— Third Public Performance at the Shanghai Theatre

Following Fudan's "Compromise" and the amateur actors' "Imperial Envoy," now there is the Shanghai Theatre's "Chocolate Girl."

The reason for staging "Chocolate Girl" is probably because comedy is easy to please the audience and attract the audience, right? "Compromise" and "Imperial Envoy" had a lot of audiences, didn't they? But can something with only laughter and no satire be considered a comedy?

When Mr. Chen Dabei was the "exclusive manager" of the Shanghai Theatre, there were two public performances—"Modern Wife" and "Xi Shi." The results of those two public performances were not good: "Modern Wife" had too much of the "civilized drama" flavor; and the so-called musical drama "Xi Shi" was "improved Peking opera."

This time, Mr. Xiang Peiliang has joined. Mr. Xiang usually has at least some research on drama. Therefore, although the previous two performances of the Shanghai Theatre have disappointed me, this time, I still have the courage to watch their third public performance.

However, I am very disappointed. "Chocolate Girl" still gives me a disappointment. — This time, although Mr. Xiang Peiliang is the stage director.

I have not read the script of "Chocolate Girl." I don't even know if there is a Chinese translation. Therefore, I have no way of knowing whether the so-called "adapted by Mr. Chen Dabei" is adapted from the original French, or translated from another language, or adapted from a Chinese translation.

From the intuition gained on the stage, the script of "Chocolate Girl" should be very light, as light as the name suggests, like a chocolate candy that young ladies and young masters love to eat when they are idle.

— Yes, the performance significance of "Chocolate Girl" is only to whet the appetite of young ladies and young masters when they read and watch it. Here it tells you about a "pampered young lady who no one has ever dared to disobey. She is tired of this life. She wants to find a strong man. Paul is very disgusted with her because she is impolite. But disgust will attract attention, and attention will lead to love." It tells you "scolding is love, hitting is flirting." It tells you "Paul lost his marriage and his job, and hates the chocolate girl to the bone. But there is love in hate, and he unconsciously loves the chocolate girl in his heart." — You see, isn't this so-called "comedy" just right for young masters and young ladies to peel chocolate candies and watch?

In terms of performance, "Chocolate Girl" is not as relaxed as the script. Although the laughter is often heard in the audience because of the rich laughter of the script structure (just laughter), those laughs are caused by the script, not by any special skills of the director. — To laugh, the antics of Wheeler and Woolsey, who are famous for their nonsense, will make you laugh even more.

Speaking of the acting skills of the actors, Miss Cheng Jingzi's "Chocolate Girl" is still acceptable, but not noble enough. Because of the lack of nobility, the impression she gives me is just a spoiled little girl acting coquettish. (This is because of the lack of life experience and understanding of the role, which is even more revealed in the lack of grasp of personality in the fourth act). Next, Li Chen, who plays the painter Fei Lixiang, can be counted. Although he is too slick, somewhat close to the slick young men in "foreign-style new dramas," he is still more oily and closer to the clowns in foreign-style new dramas than the gentleman who plays the coachman. However, Li Chen's more natural movements and speech are much better than the stiff mechanical movements of others. Bai Xiongfei, who plays Paul, and Liu Xinzhu, who plays "Chocolate Sister," have movements and speech that are close to mechanical. Chen Dabei, who plays the father of "Chocolate Girl," and Zhu Renhe, who plays the father of Fu Jie, sometimes tighten their throats, and sometimes restore their original voices. The kind of stiff and excessive movements are very annoying.

The makeup of the actors is also not good, and the dark circles around the eyes are a common phenomenon.

What is more commendable is the color of the scenery. The light blue and light yellow colors are very suitable for such a light script. Although the colors in the first two acts are too earthy, and other aspects are also lacking in realism, the use of light colors to match the lighthearted play gives people a sense of lightness, which is good after all.

Raft 224

— Laoxin

— A Story of the Sea

The small steamer seemed a little overwhelmed, dragging our cargo ships into the Yuan River with great effort.

The four of us muttered inwardly, complaining that the damn machine and light bulb were not working properly, dragging us along like an earthworm, as slow as if it hadn't eaten for seven or eight days. It was already dusk, the sun had fled, and if we didn't hurry to the dock, we would have to wait until tomorrow morning to clear customs. Damn it, clearing customs takes half a day, are we going to play mahjong on New Year's Day tomorrow?

"If we don't make it, I'll kill that opium smoker. This year's New Year is already a bit unlucky, and we still have to be so tired that we can't even celebrate the New Year, that's really unbelievable."

Third Uncle was also anxious, biting on his long pipe. We knew that when we went to other places, this old guy would watch the boat alone. But this time, coming to Wuzhou won't work. He has a relative on Jiufang Street, whether it's a sworn brother or a godson, who is his old flame. This time, he's also running into the New Year. Isn't he going to play a happy game of tianjiu or pai gow? It's a bit like what Lao Qi said—"The old man's heart is not old, turtle!" Who isn't the same?

We could already see the high place that looked like a turret. We also put down a worry.

"Draw ghost legs, treat us to a midnight snack, damn it if you don't come!"

I asked them with a bit of provocation. Although it would take half a day for the cargo ship to dock, the feeling of being extremely constrained was already relieved.

"Come on! Damn it if you don't come! I say: two for two cents, one for four cents, and one is free! How about it?"

Lao Qi was happily chattering, but Third Uncle put on a stern face. —

"Happy? Happy your ass, you guys! The boat hasn't docked yet..."

We were all sensible. Before he could scold us outright, we all stood up. Lao Gui untied the towline, and Wu Shu and I each held one side of the boat steadily, and then we used poles to push it to the dock. At this time, everyone was silent, everyone was quickly pushing, and everyone was full of hope.

The cargo ship docked on the Renhe raft. The crew on the raft were all old friends. After greeting each other, we arranged all the necessary procedures. The cargo couldn't be unloaded tonight, so we let it sit for a day. Third Uncle changed into a silk gown and walked ashore with a sway. We distributed the work, gathered some small money, left Wu Shu to watch the boat, and the three of us whistled and jumped ashore to "shop."

We hadn't been ashore for seven or eight days, and we felt a bit curious. It seemed that everything was so new, and it was also the end of the year. The streets were noisy with firecrackers and thunderclaps, which startled us like "Grandma Liu entering the Grand View Garden." We didn't know whether to laugh or shout loudly to our heart's content. Lao Qi was a weirdo. He looked at some women dressed like characters on the stage, with faces like monkey butts, and walking like chives twisting and turning. He seemed mesmerized, and used various methods to tease them, looking for happiness. Lao Gui and I found it both funny and annoying. We couldn't find a reason, we didn't know who was wrong or who was right? So, although we bought five pounds of wujiapi wine, half a roast duck, plus some braised dishes, lettuce, fish, and the like, and were ready to rush back to the boat, Lao Qi was still so reluctant to leave. Finally, I slapped him hard and said to him:

"After drinking half a pound, let's go hunting, okay?"

He laughed, and we laughed too. It was the New Year, and we didn't want anyone to fall out with anyone.

Getting off the raft, the raft drifted on the water, and we climbed up a shadow again, remembering the terribleness of life at sea—

"Damn you for three generations, working hard even during the New Year! The money we earn is still spent by that damn guy alone, inviting those sworn brothers to Chen Tang, or taking a few red-card girls to the streets. We're afraid of losing to them! If it weren't for that, we would be celebrating the New Year at home, I really don't know how happy we would be, damn it!"

Our lives are like these rafts made of wood. Three hundred and sixty-five days a year, we spend every day on the water. — "We make a living from the water!" The crew on the Renhe raft treated us as old friends, but we were most afraid of him mentioning Lao Liu. Last Dragon Boat Festival we were still together, now—

"Damn you, if you talk any more, I'll cut off your necks. Lao Liu was born on the water and died on the water, so what?",

In order to easily forget some things, we poured the wujiapi wine into our throats like tea, until we forgot how much we had drunk. I was the first to stand up, a little crazy, with a blurry mind. Our ears only heard everyone raising their voices and singing those messy little tunes:

"Half a chicken, a pot of Yongliwei wine, I walked forward and knelt down,..."

Special Feature

A Visit to the Chiba Soy Sauce Business in Japan (5) 226

— (Ye Xiyuan)

I will now excerpt from my diary of the visit at that time:

On June 8th, I took the Joban Line from Ueno Station to Kashiwa Station, then took the local Sobu Line to Noda Station to visit the 17th Factory of Noda Soy Sauce Co., Ltd. I was received and guided by the Manufacturing Department Manager, Mr. Namiki Shigetaro, to visit the various manufacturing rooms: (A) Raw Material Warehouse, using vacuum tubes to transport the soybeans to the refining room for sorting out the good and the bad. The soybeans are put into a washing machine and then transferred to a soybean steaming pot; each pot can hold ten stones of soybeans and takes three hours to steam. The wheat is put into a wheat roasting machine and then transferred to a wheat crushing machine; one machine can roast and crush five stones of wheat per hour. The soybeans and wheat are then transported to the corridor in front of the koji room, mixed with koji seeds, placed in the koji frame, and moved into the koji room to adjust the temperature. After three days, the koji is ready, and salt water is added. It is then transported to the fermentation tank (made of reinforced concrete—what the Japanese call the "Moromi Storage Room" or "Preparation Warehouse"—each concrete tank can hold 100 stones of "Moromi"). Then, it is stirred with air, and after seventeen months, it is transported to a hydraulic press to press the soy sauce. The soybean fat is extracted to make pure soy sauce, and then it is simmered in a cauldron, which is called "Fire Entry" the next day, to mature the soy sauce. It is then transported to the packaging room for packaging. The 17th Factory started construction in March of the 11th year of the Taisho era and was completed in December of the 14th year of the Taisho era, taking three and a half years to build. The construction cost a total of 10 million yen, the total area of the site is 20,000 tsubo, the total area of the buildings is 13,000 tsubo, and the brewing capacity is 150,000 koku. The completeness of its equipment and the grand scale are truly astonishing. After the tour, we went to the Kofu-kai (Community Center) to rest. The company provided 600,000 yen as a foundation, which enabled it to be well managed. It has a lecture hall, an auditorium, a social room, a library, a dining room, and a cooking room, all in good order. After sitting for a while, Mr. Mogi Saheiji, the managing director of the company, came to talk, and then Mr. Mogi invited us to a banquet at the Kofu-kai... It is said that the company produces more than 500,000 koku of soy sauce annually, accounting for more than 20% of the total national soy sauce production in Japan. In addition to being sold in Japan, Korea, and Manchuria, it is also exported to Southeast Asia, the archipelagoes, and the Americas, Canada, and Brazil...."

Broadcasting

Radio Drama Script "Temptation" 227

Old Wu: They've been here too, a big guy came, fat like a pig! Before he even said a word, he started panting, I was really scared by him at the time, I thought he was going to hit someone!

Little Lu: He came to our place too. We didn't think he was going to hit anyone, but we were afraid, his panting was like having an epileptic fit. Later we told him that the harvest wasn't very good this year, the rice shops in the city sell it cheaply, so the buying price has also been reduced, and the land rent and taxes are so high. To be honest, sometimes we don't even have rice to eat from our own fields, where would we get the money to pay the land rent!

Old Wu: So what did he say?

Little Lu: They are really ruthless. That fat pig said, if you don't have cash, grain is also acceptable.

Old Wu: So didn't he hear you say that you don't even have food, so where would you get grain?

Little Lu: Those many heartless beasts, they don't understand human feelings. They don't care about that, and finally, with a stern face, they told us: if you don't deliver it to the bureau in a week, we will send a large number of people to arrest you and take you to court!

Old Wu: Alas! We'll just have to go to court then, we're not rich enough to refuse to pay the rent!

Little Lu: Yes! Screw them, we'll just have to wait and see this year! So, what did he do to you?

Old Wu: Damn it, that big guy had someone tie up our 180-jin sow and take it away!

Little Lu: (Laughing loudly) It can be matched with him! (Both laugh loudly)

A Qiao: (Calling from a distance) Little Lu, come and eat, if you don't come, we'll eat it all.

Little Lu: (Responding) Coming, Old Wu, have you eaten?

Old Wu: I've eaten, go and eat quickly? Come back and chat after you're full.

Little Lu: Let's go to our place, watch us eat, and chat for a while, okay? Let's go, let's go. (Runs off)

Elder Brother: Why didn't you come and eat earlier? You're always playing when you're young!

Old Wu: We weren't playing, we were chatting there, Elder Brother, you eat yours!

Elder Brother: Old Wu, have you eaten? Just eat with us here, so you don't have to bother going back.

Old Wu: I ate a long time ago, you guys eat quickly; it'll get cold later.

A Qiao: Isn't it too hot to eat, why are you so silly? (Everyone laughs, sound of bowls and chopsticks)

Elder Brother: (Saying while eating) After this meal, I don't know where we'll eat the next one.

A Qiao: Who says there isn't a lot of rice left in the bucket?

Elder Brother: (Sneering) There is enough rice to eat for a few more meals, but... (Everyone is silent)

Little Lu: But what? Elder Brother, tell us!

Old Wu: Is it about that big fat guy?

Little Lu: If we have to go to court, I'll go. What's so strange about that? If the year is bad, it's not bad to go inside and live a peaceful life.

Elder Brother: It's not about that, let's eat, we'll talk about it later even if there is something!

A Qiao: What exactly is going on? Elder Brother, are we in danger?

Little Lu: Of course there's danger, otherwise why would Elder Brother be so worried?

Old Wu: I know, is it about the flooding in Shang County?

Elder Brother: That's right, a group of refugees just passed by here, I asked them about the flood situation in Shang County...

(2)
